Snape contributed to the defences set up around the magical artefact by adding a Potions Riddle as one of the obstacles, and the only obstacle that used logic as a key factor instead of magic.<sup id="cite_ref-PS16_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS16-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> At the same time, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> became a student in Snape's classes, and the two of them detested each other almost immediately. Harry's resemblance to <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">his father</a> and his acquired 'celebrity' status brought the worst out of Snape from their very first <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> lesson.<sup id="cite_ref-PS8_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS8-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Although Snape had pledged an oath to Dumbledore that he would protect Harry, such an oath did not stand in the way of Snape's bias to Slytherin House, nor did it mean Harry was to get any special treatment in academics.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Throughout the year as part of his promise to Dumbledore, Snape did everything he could to prevent <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Professor Quirinus Quirrell</a> from helping <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> obtain the Philosopher's Stone, having seen him as what he was and at least knew he was helping Voldemort, if not also being aware of Voldemort possessing Quirell. By <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">31 October</a>, the turbaned Professor, sure enough, made his first move by letting a <a href="/wiki/Mountain_troll" title="Mountain troll">Mountain troll</a> into <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> as a diversion. Snape took this chance to stop him from sneaking into the <a href="/wiki/Third-floor_corridor" title="Third-floor corridor">restricted third-floor corridor</a> where the Stone was being hidden in the midst of the chaotic event, only to get bitten in the leg by the corridor's <a href="/wiki/Three-headed_dog" title="Three-headed dog">three-headed guard dog</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fluffy" title="Fluffy">Fluffy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS10_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS10-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-PS17_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS17-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811182354" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150811182354" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811182354" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150811182354" decoding="async" width="240" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20150811182354" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-disneyscreencaps.com-10067.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape saving Harry's life during a Quidditch game</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Quirrell made his first attempt on Harry's life by <a href="/wiki/Broom_jinx" title="Broom jinx">jinxing</a> <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter%27s_Nimbus_2000" title="Harry Potter&#39;s Nimbus 2000">his new broomstick</a> during the boy's first <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> game, Snape intervened again by performing a <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">counter-curse</a> to prevent Harry from being hurled off. Unfortunately, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> observed the crowd through binoculars to figure out who was performing the jinx and caught Snape discreetly uttering the counter-curse incantation, but erroneously thought he was performing the actual curse. So she ran to his stand and <a href="/wiki/Bluebell_Flames" title="Bluebell Flames">set fire</a> to his robes in order to distract him and make him stop, and luckily for Snape, she accidentally knocked Quirrell over during her hurry back to the Gryffindor stands, causing him to break the eye contact necessary for performing his spell correctly. For the next match, Snape insisted on refereeing to make sure it did not happen again. This did not come across well to the other teachers, who believed that he was just trying to injure the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>'s chances of winning.<sup id="cite_ref-PS11_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS11-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 266px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest?cb=20131016224556" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="264" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape and quirrell.png" data-image-key="Snape_and_quirrell.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20131016224556" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest?cb=20131016224556" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20131016224556" decoding="async" width="264" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape and quirrell.png" data-image-key="Snape_and_quirrell.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Snape_and_quirrell.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/264?cb=20131016224556" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_and_quirrell.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape confronting Quirrell during the night</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape intensely confronted Quirrell in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> on the night after the match, demanding to know why he was after the Philosopher's Stone. Unbeknownst to them both, Harry was watching the entire argument from the treetops, having followed his Potions teacher into the forest on his broomstick after passing him at the school <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_Changing_Rooms" title="Quidditch Changing Rooms">Quidditch shed</a>. But because the boy suspected Snape of plotting to steal the stone and of attempting to kill him, it seemed to him that the Potions professor was trying to intimidate Quirrell into handing over information regarding the artefact.<sup id="cite_ref-PS13_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS13-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> So he, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and Hermione unjustly tried to be supportive and encouraging to Quirrell whenever possible by telling people off for laughing at his stutter, smiling at him encouragingly whenever they passed him or arguing with Snape.<sup id="cite_ref-PS14_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS14-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Snape was present at the <a href="/wiki/End-of-Term_Feast" title="End-of-Term Feast">End-of-Term Feast</a> that year. He was initally very pleased to see that Slytherin had won the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a> again, but was forced to shake McGonagall's hand with a forced smile after Dumbledore's additional house points to Harry, Ron, Hermione and Nevile meant that Gryffindor had won instead.<sup id="cite_ref-PS17_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS17-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1992-1993_school_year">1992-1993 school year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1992-1993 school year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 1992-1993 school year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Maybe he's left, because he missed out on the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> job again!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley </b>: "<i>Or he might have been sacked! I mean, everyone hates him —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Or maybe he's waiting to hear why you two didn't arrive on the school train.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Confronting Harry and Ron after they arrive via a flying car<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 246px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Harry%2C_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape%27s_office.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170703224045" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="244" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry, Ron and Filch in Snape&#39;s office.jpg" data-image-key="Harry,_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape&#39;s_office.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Harry%2C_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape%27s_office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20170703224045" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Harry%2C_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape%27s_office.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170703224045" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Harry%2C_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape%27s_office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20170703224045" decoding="async" width="244" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry, Ron and Filch in Snape&#39;s office.jpg" data-image-key="Harry,_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape&#39;s_office.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Harry%2C_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape%27s_office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20170703224045" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry,_Ron_and_Filch_in_Snape%27s_office.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry Potter and Ron Weasley in Snape's office after being seen by Muggles driving a flying Ford Anglia</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the beginning of the school year in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Snape learned from the <i><a href="/wiki/Evening_Prophet" title="Evening Prophet">Evening Prophet</a></i> that Muggles spotted Harry and Ron travelling to Hogwarts in a <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">flying Ford Anglia</a>, instead of on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. Knowing the severity of their deeds could very well cause them to be expelled, which would put Harry in great danger as he would lose Dumbledore's protection, Snape took matters into his hand and confronted them when they had landed, where he severely berated them for their breach of one of the most sacred laws of their world and pretended to call upon Professors Dumbledore and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> to make them solve this situation. It was as Snape wanted: Dumbledore ensured they would not be expelled and Minerva punished them instead by giving them a warning and separate detentions.<sup id="cite_ref-COS5_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS5-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Regardless of his desire to uphold Lily's memory, Snape considered the punishment too lenient and retaliated by allowing the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin Quidditch team</a> to unfairly usurp the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Quidditch_pitch" title="Hogwarts Quidditch pitch">Hogwarts Quidditch pitch</a> during the Gryffindor team's practice time. This was in order for them to train <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> as their new <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS7_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS7-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Later on in the year, Harry, Ron, and Hermione successfully managed to smuggle <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> ingredients from Snape's personal cabinets. They did this by creating a spectacle of a diversion in his classroom, which involved a firecracker and the <a href="/wiki/Swelling_Solution" title="Swelling Solution">Swelling Solution</a> that was being made in class. He was utterly furious at the mess and the way he looked it Harry made it clear he knew it was Harry who had caused it considering the way he looked at Harry, with Harry referring to having felt Snape read his mind, strongly indicating Snape used <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a> on him.<sup id="cite_ref-COS11_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS11-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> However, he was forced to let Harry go again as Dumbledore had made it clear to him that no other punishment but being expelled would be dealt out to Harry if he broke another rule and Snape could not let his anger overpower his desire to see Lily's son be protected.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718022052" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718022052" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718022052" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718022052" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718022052" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-movie-duel.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape prepares to duel Lockhart during the first and last Duelling Club meeting</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Time to split up the dream team, I think. Weasley, you can partner Finnigan. Potter — I don’t think so. Mr Malfoy, come over here. Let’s see what you make of the famous Potter. And you, Miss Granger — you can partner <a href="/wiki/Millicent_Bulstrode" title="Millicent Bulstrode">Miss Bulstrode</a>.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape running the Duelling Club<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>During this year, Professor Snape also worked with the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, in running the <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a>. In this period, he quickly visibly showed a large amount of irritation and anger at Professor Lockhart who would remain, evermore, the teacher of the subject he most cherished. Snape took a certain amount of enjoyment in blasting him against a wall with the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> and looking ready to murder him on the spot to the point that even Lockhart was intimidated enough to stop annoying Snape. He ensured that Harry would be engaged with Draco instead, but interfered when Harry and Draco practically checkmated each other, with Harry using the <a href="/wiki/Tickling_Charm" title="Tickling Charm">Tickling Charm</a> on Malfoy and was subsequently hit by the <a href="/wiki/Dancing_Feet_Spell" title="Dancing Feet Spell">Dancing Feet Spell</a>. Although he gave Malfoy the instruction needed to <a href="/wiki/Snake_Summons_Spell" title="Snake Summons Spell">conjure a snake</a> and relished the fact that Harry was alone to face the large angry <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a>, once Harry showed his <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a> ability, Snape quickly interfered to avoid too much of a problem on Harry's part by <a href="/wiki/Snake-Vanishing_Spell" title="Snake-Vanishing Spell">vanishing</a> the snake and allowing him to be escorted out of the Great Hall by his friends but looked at him suspiciously before he left.<sup id="cite_ref-COS11_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS11-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Lockhart would only further irritate Professor Snape during <a href="/wiki/Valentine%27s_Day" title="Valentine&#39;s Day">Valentine's Day</a>, where he held a party to celebrate it as Snape looked on particularly dreadfully to the point he looked as if he had been forced to take multiple <a href="/wiki/Skele-Gro" title="Skele-Gro">Skele-Gro</a> and Snape did not hesitate to look utterly infuriated when Lockhart cheerfully asked the students to make Snape brew for them <a href="/wiki/Love_Potion" class="mw-redirect" title="Love Potion">Love Potions</a> to the point he clearly shot a warning look to them that he would force-feed anyone who dared to ask him to <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poison</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS13_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS13-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Snape was very likely among the professors who were highly irritated by the Cupids Lockhart unleashed upon Hogwarts as they keep getting in the way of lessons. This hatred for Lockhart finally reached its apex when Professor Lockhart walked in upon their discovery of Ginny being taken to the Chamber of Secrets, as even Snape was genuinely concerned for her regardless of how he treated Gryffindor, and furiously led the teachers into forcing him out of the way so that students could be escorted to safety, outright not giving Lockhart even a second to rebuke Snape's claim of having heard Lockhart proclaim that he had found the monster.<sup id="cite_ref-COS16_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS16-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Snape was also responsible for the brewing of the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a> in order to cure all those <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrificatied</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Serpent_of_Slytherin" title="Serpent of Slytherin">Serpent of Slytherin</a> that terrorised the school that year.<sup id="cite_ref-COS9_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS9-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By describing the <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> in Potions class (which Hermione remembered), and demonstrating the Disarming Charm to the Duelling Club, Snape taught Harry two skills that ultimately proved critical to his success.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1993-1994_school_year">1993-1994 school year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1993-1994 school year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 1993-1994 school year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Well, well, well, I never thought I'd meet a third-year class who wouldn't even recognise a <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">werewolf</a> when they saw one. I shall make a point of informing Professor Dumbledore how very behind you all are.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape substituting as the DADA professor<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><p>During this school year, Snape demonstrated his expertise with potions by brewing the complex <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> for the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>. Throughout this year, Snape suspected that Lupin may be helping <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, an escapee from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, enter Hogwarts castle. This suspicion stemmed from Lupin's friendship with Sirius and Harry's father <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> when they were all at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as students. It is revealed that Sirius once played a joke on Snape, telling him that he could find out where Lupin was going every month if he climbed into the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>. James realised the danger and saved Snape's life by pulling him back.
</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Snape%2C_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811180558" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="114" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape, Sirius and Remus in the Shrieking Shack.jpg" data-image-key="Snape,_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Snape%2C_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150811180558" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Snape%2C_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811180558" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Snape%2C_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150811180558" decoding="async" width="245" height="114" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape, Sirius and Remus in the Shrieking Shack.jpg" data-image-key="Snape,_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Snape%2C_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150811180558" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape,_Sirius_and_Remus_in_the_Shrieking_Shack.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape confronts Sirius and Lupin in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Near the end of the school year, Snape ambushed Black as he entered the school again and attempted to apprehend him, believing him to have been the one who had betrayed Lily to Voldemort. Snape appeared from under the <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a> that Harry had left near the Whomping Willow, tied Remus up, and while engaged in a vociferous argument with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and Hermione, he attempted to arrange to send Sirius and Remus to Azkaban Prison. However, before he could give Sirius and Remus to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, Harry, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> simultaneously used Expelliarmus on Snape. Snape also said that Harry, Ron, and Hermione faced suspension for being out-of-bounds. Since Harry aided Black's escape, Snape was beside himself with indignation. On the last day of school, he revealed to his students that Lupin was a werewolf, forcing Lupin to resign his post.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1994-1995_school_year">1994-1995 school year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1994-1995 school year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 1994-1995 school year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"'<i>Course Dumbledore trusts you. He's a trusting man, isn't he? Believes in second chances. But me — I say there are spots that don't come off, Snape. <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark#On_the_arm" title="Dark Mark">Spots that never come off</a>, d'you know what I mean?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> <span class="template-c">(as Alastor Moody)</span> referring to Snape's Dark Mark<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Harry%27s_choosing_confusion.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160114192835" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s choosing confusion.jpg" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_choosing_confusion.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Harry%27s_choosing_confusion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160114192835" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Harry%27s_choosing_confusion.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160114192835" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Harry%27s_choosing_confusion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160114192835" decoding="async" width="251" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry&#39;s choosing confusion.jpg" data-image-key="Harry&#39;s_choosing_confusion.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Harry%27s_choosing_confusion.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20160114192835" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry%27s_choosing_confusion.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape and others' reactions after Harry Potter is selected as the fourth Triwizard champion</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape was apoplectic when Harry's name was unexpectedly chosen from the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a>. Despite the fishy circumstances surrounding the incident and the immense dangers that Harry was facing, Snape refused to believe that he did not deliberately enter himself in for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. Indeed, he continued to treat Harry as maliciously as ever, thinking that he had broken into his office to steal ingredients that would aid him in the underwater phase of the tournament.
</p><p>Harry later discovered that Snape was once a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> but had been vouched for by Dumbledore. Dumbledore told the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> that although Snape had indeed worked for Voldemort, he changed sides and turned spy against him. Dumbledore reassured Harry that Snape's loyalties were genuine, though he refused to tell Harry why.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF30_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF30-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry was not the only one who had expressed scepticism over Snape's reform. <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Professor Moody</a> had Snape's office searched at the beginning of the year, claiming that it was an "Auror's privilege" and that Dumbledore mentioned being watchful of him. Snape was resentful of Moody's accusations but could not do anything about it. (In truth, Moody was actually an impostor who had been raiding Snape's cabinet for ingredients to make <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a>.)
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718015710" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170718015710" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718015710" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170718015710" decoding="async" width="251" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20170718015710" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-12913.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Karkaroff</a> showing Snape his Dark Mark</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite Snape's unawareness of the real reason why Harry was in the tournament, it had not escaped his notice that Lord Voldemort's mark was becoming increasingly more pronounced throughout the year. Karkaroff, who dreaded retribution from Voldemort, panicked and confided his fears in Snape. Karkaroff attempted to talk to him numerous times throughout the year, but Snape had no sympathy for him and offered no help. Karkaroff consequently fled when the Dark Lord returned, but Snape, who remained in the Dark Lord's good favour with the information he could provide on Dumbledore, had nothing to fear from him in the term of retribution. In fact, he appeared to have been waiting for Voldemort's return more than ever in this year, as he and Dumbledore were conversing about it.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape uses his Dark Mark as proof that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> has returned</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament#The_Third_Task" title="Triwizard Tournament">Third Task</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Return_of_Lord_Voldemort" title="Return of Lord Voldemort">Rebirth of Lord Voldemort</a>, Barty Crouch Jnr took Harry to Moody's office. Crouch Jnr started to question Harry about what had happened but was shortly rescued by Professors Dumbledore, McGonagall, and Snape. Soon the effects of Crouch Jnr's Polyjuice Potion wore off; in the excitement, he had neglected to take it at the proper time to maintain his cover. Under the effects of <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> provided by Professor Snape, Crouch described Lord Voldemort's plan to resurrect himself and Crouch Jnr's own involvement in getting Harry to the graveyard. Dumbledore and Snape attempted to convince a disbelieving <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> that Voldemort had returned. Snape was finally told the truth about Sirius's innocence and was forced by Dumbledore to shake hands. He was subsequently sent on a secret mission by Dumbledore to rejoin the Death Eaters and spy on the Dark Lord as a re-doubled agent.
</p>
<h3><span id="Second_Wizarding_War_(1995-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_Wizarding_War_.281995-1998.29">Second Wizarding War <span class="template-c">(1995-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Second Wizarding War (1995-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1995-1996_school_year">1995-1996 school year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1995-1996 school year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 1995-1996 school year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>I wish to interrogate him! I wish you to provide me with a potion that will force him to tell me the truth!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>I have already told you, that I have no further stocks of Veritaserum. Unless you wish to poison Potter — and I assure you I would have the greatest sympathy with you if you did — I cannot help you. The only trouble is that most venoms act too fast to give the victim much time for truth-telling....</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape witholding Veritaserum from Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>During the 1995-1996 school year, with Voldemort having returned to his body, Snape carried on with his work as a re-doubled agent for Dumbledore. During the summer, he was seen at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> giving reports to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Snape frequently taunted Sirius about the latter not being able to take an active role in the Order's missions due to his fugitive status.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161121214826" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121214826" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161121214826" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121214826" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121214826" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-8309.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry's first Occlumency lesson with Snape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Back at school, Snape's allegiance to the Order had no effect on his dislike for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>. When Harry began having visions about Lord Voldemort, Dumbledore asked Snape to teach Harry <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> in order to shut down the telepathic connection.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> However, mutual hostility made it difficult for them to work productively during the sessions. Indeed, Snape had to be very careful in the ways that he helped Harry, should Voldemort read Harry's mind and discover his servant working against him. At one point, Harry peeked into the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a> when Snape was out of his office and witnessed a private memory of Snape being viciously bullied and harassed by <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">Harry's father</a>. Upon returning, Snape grabbed him roughly by the arm and threw him out of the office and forbade him from ever coming back again. For all the rest of that semester, he treated Harry with redoubled contempt and fury and ignored him in class whenever possible. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180203175328" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180203175328" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><span><i>"</i></span><i>He's got <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Padfoot</a> at the place where it's hidden.<span>"</span></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Towards the end of the school year, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> captured Harry and questioned him on the whereabouts of Dumbledore. She sent for Snape to provide <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> to force Harry to reveal any information he may be hiding. Snape claimed that his supplies of Veritaserum were exhausted earlier, when she had attempted to use the drug surreptitiously to force information from Harry (however, it is highly likely that he lied). As a result, Snape withheld further assistance.
</p><p>It is later revealed that Snape had actually given Umbridge a fake potion during her prior attempts. Upon hearing Harry's cryptic warning about Sirius's capture, he swiftly carried the message back to the other Order members, and helped come up with a plan for them to come to the rescue in the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a> while he searched the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> for Harry. But since Umbridge was near, he pretended to ignore it. However, despite the fact that Snape came to his aid multiple times throughout the year, Harry hated him as much as ever, due to believing that Snape's goading spurred Sirius into joining the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">battle</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="1996-1997_school_year">1996-1997 school year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 1996-1997 school year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 1996-1997 school year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Well, there’s one good thing. Snape’ll be gone by the end of the year.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>What do you mean?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>That job’s jinxed. No ones lasted more than a year...Quirrell actually died doing it...Personally, I’m going to keep my fingers crossed for another death...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Harry Potter's reaction to Snape becoming the Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140918121231" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="108" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Unbreakable vow.gif" data-image-key="Unbreakable_vow.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140918121231" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140918121231" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140918121231" decoding="async" width="245" height="108" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Unbreakable vow.gif" data-image-key="Unbreakable_vow.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/Unbreakable_vow.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140918121231" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unbreakable_vow.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> making an Unbreakable Vow, with Bellatrix Lestrange as the bonding agent</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In July 1996 Dumbledore had been afflicted by a <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">powerful curse</a> cast on <a href="/wiki/Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" class="mw-redirect" title="Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">Marvolo Gaunt's ring</a>, one of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, prior to the start of Harry's sixth year at Hogwarts. Although Snape's knowledge of the Dark Arts enabled him to slow the spread of the curse, the curse would have ultimately killed Dumbledore within a year. Dumbledore, aware that Voldemort had ordered Draco to kill him, asked Snape to kill him instead as a way of sparing the boy's soul and of preventing his own otherwise slow, painful death. Although Snape was reluctant, even asking about the impact of such an action on his own soul, Dumbledore implied that this kind of coup de grâce would not damage a human's <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a> in the same way murder would. Furthermore, once Snape had done the deed, he would gain Voldemort's complete trust and learn more of his plans. Snape agreed to do as the Headmaster requested.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly after that, Snape was visited by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> and <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a> at his home in <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner&#39;s End">Spinner's End</a>. Narcissa's son <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco</a> had been given a difficult task by Voldemort, and Narcissa swore Snape to an <a href="/wiki/Unbreakable_Vow" title="Unbreakable Vow">Unbreakable Vow</a>, on pain of death should he break it, that he would protect Draco, help him complete Voldemort's task, and finish the task himself if Draco failed. When questioned by Bellatrix about his loyalties, Snape claimed to have been working for Voldemort (rather than for Dumbledore) ever since Voldemort's return, and explained his actions in the previous years in that light. In addition, he pointed out that Dumbledore's protection had kept him out of <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and free to operate on Voldemort's behalf.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP2_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP2-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the start-of-term feast at Hogwarts, Dumbledore announced he had finally appointed Snape as Professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, much to Harry's shock and displeasure.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP8_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP8-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> Snape was no less severe in teaching Defence than he had been with Potions, although he did allow students who achieved below "Outstanding" at <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> level to enter his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a> classes. Having finally acquired the position he desired for so long, Snape taught the lessons with a tone of passion for the Dark Arts he sought to undo, something he did not do for Potions.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_27-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> He also became less biased, as he allowed Hermione to answer his question<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_27-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> (as opposed to three years ago, he insulted her for being "an insufferable know-it-all"),<sup id="cite_ref-POA9_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA9-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> and sentenced Crabbe and Goyle to detention for dissatisfying progress in their repeated <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">fifth year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP15_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP15-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190209142010" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="SeverusSnape WB F6 SnapeAndDracoInHallway Still 080615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142010" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190209142010" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142010" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="SeverusSnape WB F6 SnapeAndDracoInHallway Still 080615 Land.jpg" data-image-key="SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190209142010" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SeverusSnape_WB_F6_SnapeAndDracoInHallway_Still_080615_Land.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape offering Draco Malfoy assistance with his mission</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, a retired Hogwarts teacher, replaced Snape as Potions Master. Slughorn loaned Harry an <a href="/wiki/Half-Blood_Prince%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" class="mw-redirect" title="Half-Blood Prince&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">old Potions textbook</a>, in which Harry found marginalia including helpful tips on how to make potions better,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_27-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and a variety of curious spells seemingly invented by an unknown student.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP12_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP12-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> The book was inscribed "<i>This Book is the Property of the Half-Blood Prince</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_27-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> With the help of the notes, Harry quickly became the best potion-maker in the class and Slughorn's favourite student. Snape, however, was suspicious when he heard about Harry's newfound success, maintaining that he <i>"never had the impression that [he] had been able to teach Potter anything at all</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-HBP15_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP15-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the spring, Snape met with Dumbledore on the outskirts of the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> and wanted to know more about the private lessons between Albus and Harry. Not knowing that they were overheard by Hagrid, Snape burst into resentment that Dumbledore trusts Harry more than him. Dumbledore only ordered Severus to look after Draco even more, after <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> has been poisoned. Albus also invited him for an evening visit in <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Headmaster&#39;s office">his office</a>. When Snape arrived and learned that Harry had to die, he showed outrage and ultimately showed that he still after all these years loved <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a> by revealing his <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to be a doe, the same as Lily's.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20100811181504" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vulnera Sanentur.JPG" data-image-key="Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100811181504" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20100811181504" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100811181504" decoding="async" width="220" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vulnera Sanentur.JPG" data-image-key="Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cb/Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20100811181504" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vulnera_Sanentur.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape healing Draco's wounds</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, in a fight with Draco, Harry cast one of the Prince's spells marked "For Enemies" (<i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>) and was horrified when it caused devastating wounds to Draco's face and chest. Snape rushed to the scene and <a href="/wiki/Vulnera_Sanentur" title="Vulnera Sanentur">healed Draco's wounds</a>, and then interrogated Harry about the source of the spell. When Harry refused to tell him anything, Snape demanded that he bring him all of his books. Harry hid the Prince's book and gave Ron Weasley's copy of the book to Snape instead. Snape punished Harry by giving him a detention every Saturday for the rest of the year, including during the final <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match of the season. Fearing of exposing himself as the inventor of the curse that injured Draco, Snape did not outright expose Harry's cheating in Potions to Slughorn or the rest of the staff, thus resulting in a punishment much more lenient than usual, which Professor McGonagall saw as something very lucky for Harry.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP24_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP24-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>Severus... please....</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Avada Kedavra!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape killing Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore dies.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_dies.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140813154818" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140813154818" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140813154818" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore dies.gif" data-image-key="Dumbledore_dies.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a7/Dumbledore_dies.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140813154818" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_dies.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape proves his loyalty to Dumbledore - by ending the headmaster's life as requested</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before leaving with Dumbledore to find a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, Harry discovered from <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Sybill Trelawney</a> that it had been Severus who overheard the <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Prophecy</a> and told it to Voldemort, thus causing Voldemort to hunt Harry and his parents. Despite this and Harry's angry questions, Dumbledore maintained that he trusted Snape. After returning to Hogwarts with the Slytherin Locket, Harry and Dumbledore flew to the school's <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a>. Gravely weakened by Voldemort's potion, and the school being under attack by Death Eaters, Dumbledore asked Harry to fetch Snape for him. Before Harry could leave, Draco arrived and <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarmed</a> Dumbledore, intending to carry out Voldemort's ordered assassination. Draco was unable to bring himself to commit the murder, however, and Snape killed the headmaster himself.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP27_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP27-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090609234006" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape vs Harry.gif" data-image-key="Snape_vs_Harry.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090609234006" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest?cb=20090609234006" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090609234006" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape vs Harry.gif" data-image-key="Snape_vs_Harry.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Snape_vs_Harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090609234006" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_vs_Harry.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"<i>You dare use my own spells against me, Potter? It was I who invented them — I, the Half-Blood Prince!</i>"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>An enraged Harry (who had been <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">immobilised</a> by Dumbledore for his own protection and had witnessed the killing while under his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a>) chased Snape, Draco, and the Death Eaters as they fled the castle. The two of them engaged in a fierce duel, which became increasingly one-sided. Snape easily blocked Harry's attempts to attack him and jeeringly pointed out Harry's mistakes, but refused to strike back. However, he became enraged when Harry called him a coward and began using his own spells against him, resulting in him blasting Harry back against the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP28_25-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP28-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the confrontation, Snape also revealed himself to be the "Half-Blood Prince" (being the son of <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Tobias Snape</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen Prince</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a>). Harry was unable to stop Snape before the latter passed through the school gates and <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Disapparated</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP28_25-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP28-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="On_the_run">On the run</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: On the run">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: On the run"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>I don't think he wanted to associate himself with that book. I don't think Dumbledore would have liked it very much if he'd known. And even if Snape pretended it hadn't been his, Slughorn would have recognised his writing at once.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>I should have showed the book to Dumbledore. All that time he was showing me how Voldemort was evil even when he was at school, and I had proof Snape was, too —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Upon finding out Snape was the owner of the <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">textbook</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 249px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811152234" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="247" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Meeting at Malfoy Manor.jpg" data-image-key="Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20180811152234" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811152234" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20180811152234" decoding="async" width="247" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Meeting at Malfoy Manor.jpg" data-image-key="Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/247?cb=20180811152234" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus at the Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Meeting_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Meeting at Malfoy Manor">Meeting at Malfoy Manor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After killing Albus Dumbledore and fleeing the school, Snape once more rejoined the ranks of the Death Eaters. In the summer of 1997, Snape informed Lord Voldemort that Harry was to depart from his <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">relatives</a>' <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">house</a> four days before his birthday. On Dumbledore's orders, Snape told the Death Eaters the correct date so as to continue Voldemort's trust in him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH1_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH1-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Snape then fed <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a> the idea of using seven decoys of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during his movement to a place of safety so that when the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> arrived, they would not know who the real one was. In order to be consistent in his own role as a Death Eater, Snape <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">confunded</a> Fletcher so that he would not remember who told him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH1_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH1-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Because of Severus' information, when the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> moved Harry from Privet Drive they were ambushed by Death Eaters, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> ensued. During the battle, Snape accidentally sliced <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>'s ear off with <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> while aiming at another Death Eater.<sup id="cite_ref-DH5_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH5-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly after the battle, Severus visited <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> where, in <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black%27s_bedroom" title="Sirius Black&#39;s bedroom">Sirius Black' bedroom</a>, he found <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter%27s_letter" class="mw-redirect" title="Lily Potter&#39;s letter">Lily Potter's letter</a>. Snape had cut off the letter and took the page, which contained Lily's signature and love. He also cut off the picture of <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potter family</a> and took the page, which contained Lily, for himself.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="As_Headmaster">As Headmaster</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: As Headmaster">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: As Headmaster"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Severus Snape, long-standing Potions master at Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and wizardry, was today appointed Headmaster in the most important of several staffing changes at the ancient school. Following the resignation of the previous Muggle Studies teacher, Alecto Carrow will take over the post while her brother, Amycus, fills the position of Defence Against the Dark Arts professor. 'I welcome the opportunity to uphold our finest Wizarding traditions and values' —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<i>Daily Prophet</i>, <a href="/wiki/1_September" title="1 September">1 September</a>, <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140531023911" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dp severus snape.jpg" data-image-key="Dp_severus_snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140531023911" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140531023911" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140531023911" decoding="async" width="160" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dp severus snape.jpg" data-image-key="Dp_severus_snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dp_severus_snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20140531023911" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dp_severus_snape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> reports Snape's appointment as Headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the 1997-1998 school year, Snape was named Headmaster of Hogwarts, while Death Eaters <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto</a> and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> were appointed Deputy Heads. Snape used his position as Headmaster to discreetly protect the students and to contain the Carrows. It is later understood that, during his time as Headmaster, Snape consulted with the <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">portraits</a> of the previous <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmasters</a>, and continued to receive instructions from Dumbledore's portrait.
</p><p>Before the beginning of the first term, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> removed the Sword of Gryffindor from its glass case in the headmaster's office for examination, along with the other items Dumbledore left in his <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_will" class="mw-redirect" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s will">will</a>. However, this sword was a fake. The real sword had been hidden in a hole in the wall behind Dumbledore's portrait.
</p><p>When its counterfeit had been returned to Dumbledore's office, another attempt to seize the sword was made by <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>. After pretending to punish them by sending them into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> with <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, Snape passed the fake sword along to <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who kept it in her vault at <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts</a>, thinking that it was real.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140621022650" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tumblr mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3 250.gif" data-image-key="Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140621022650" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140621022650" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140621022650" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tumblr mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3 250.gif" data-image-key="Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140621022650" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tumblr_mtugozGgnm1sg49umo3_250.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry being led by a doe Patronus (Snape's Patronus) to the hiding place of the <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Sword of Gryffindor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
