<p>Upon being informed by the portrait of <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> of Harry Potter's whereabouts, Dumbledore's portrait instructed Snape to give Harry the real sword without the latter knowing it. Not only would Harry not have taken kindly to Snape's appearance after his attack on <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, and also for the murder of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> of which Harry was an eye-witness, it would have been dangerous if Voldemort were to read his mind and see Snape helping him. Snape then took the real sword, hid it in a frozen pool of water near Harry's camping spot, and used his <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to guide Harry to it. After having rescued Harry from drowning, Ron claimed to have supposedly seen someone watching from the shadows. Though not stated, it is extremely likely to have been Snape keeping an eye on Harry and only departing once he knew the latter was safe.
</p><p>As a headmaster, Snape was thoroughly disliked by many of his students. The old members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> reformed the organisation after <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> gained control over the school and started up a revolt against Snape and the Carrows. Neville Longbottom, Luna Lovegood, and Ginny Weasley were at the forefront of the rebellion. Snape, following up on his promise to Dumbledore to keep the students safe, subtly undermined the violent, sadistic attempts of the Carrows to keep control by doing things such as sending students to help <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> as punishments rather than the Carrows' more dangerous alternatives. Neville stated that Snape was hardly ever seen whilst headmaster. This could be because Snape remained in the headmaster's office most of the time or was searching for/following the trio to make sure they were safe and/or making progress. Also, during his tenure, the <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Four" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four</a> was re-enacted and students had taken to (most likely under Snape's orders) marching from point A to point B together like they were in military school.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dismissal_as_Headmaster">Dismissal as Headmaster</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dismissal as Headmaster">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Dismissal as Headmaster"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>No! You'll do no more murder at Hogwarts!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Filius Flitwick confronting Snape during his <a href="/wiki/Ousting_of_Severus_Snape" title="Ousting of Severus Snape">ousting</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110716140837" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fiery Offensive Spell.gif" data-image-key="Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110716140837" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110716140837" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110716140837" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fiery Offensive Spell.gif" data-image-key="Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110716140837" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fiery_Offensive_Spell.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape duelling McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry, Ron, and Hermione returned to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a> in search of one of the last of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, which they believed to have something to do with <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw" title="Rowena Ravenclaw">Rowena Ravenclaw</a>. The only idea they could come up with was <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s diadem">Ravenclaw's lost diadem</a>, and so Harry and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> went to the <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw_Tower" title="Ravenclaw Tower">Ravenclaw Common Room</a> to get an idea of what the diadem looked like. Here they were met by <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a>, who pressed her finger to the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a> and summoned Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH29_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH29-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a> arrived, but so did <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>.
</p><p>The two began fighting, and while Snape put up a good defence, McGonagall's attack was beginning to overwhelm him, for he was forced to take refuge behind a suit of armour when McGonagall gained the upper hand with daggers. She was soon helped by the arrival of the other Heads of House: <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Sprout</a>, <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Flitwick</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Slughorn</a>. Outnumbered, Snape fled the castle, jumping out the window of a classroom and using the ability to <a href="/wiki/Unsupported_flight" title="Unsupported flight">fly without a broom</a>, which he presumably learned from Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts_and_death"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and death</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts and death">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts and death"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>The Elder Wand cannot serve me properly, Severus, because I am not its true master. The Elder Wand belongs to the wizard who killed its last owner. You killed Albus Dumbledore. While you live, Severus, the Elder Wand cannot be truly mine</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Voldemort, explaining to Snape why he must murder him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini&#39;s_attack_on_Snape.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest?cb=20161218210623" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C32M1 Nagini&#39;s attack on Snape.png" data-image-key="B7C32M1_Nagini&#39;s_attack_on_Snape.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218210623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C32M1_Nagini%27s_attack_on_Snape.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nagini injects the venom into Snape's neck, killing him</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later in the evening, Snape was summoned by Voldemort to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. Voldemort explained that he believed that Snape was the master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a> from killing Dumbledore and that Snape must die so that the Elder Wand can be his. Snape tried to explain the situation but Voldemort ordered <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> to kill Snape by biting into his neck, injecting him with her extremely <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poisonous</a> <a href="/wiki/Nagini%27s_venom" title="Nagini&#39;s venom">venom</a>, before he could finish speaking. Before dying, Snape released a cloud of memories and told Harry, who had watched the entire scene from a hidden spot, to take them.<sup id="cite_ref-DH32_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH32-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Harry later took the memories to the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a> in Dumbledore's office. From these memories, Harry learned everything about Snape's past. In the first scene, Harry discovered that Snape had befriended Lily as a nine-year-old child when they lived near each other in the industrial town of <a href="/wiki/Cokeworth" title="Cokeworth">Cokeworth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 238px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822050346" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="236" height="133" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH2 memory Lily Evans Sorted.gif" data-image-key="DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20160822050346" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822050346" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20160822050346" decoding="async" width="236" height="133" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH2 memory Lily Evans Sorted.gif" data-image-key="DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20160822050346" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH2_memory_Lily_Evans_Sorted.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape's memory of Lily being Sorted into Gryffindor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon their arrival at Hogwarts, the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> placed Snape and Lily into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor Houses</a>, respectively. They remained close friends for the next few years until they were driven apart by Snape's interest in the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> and by Lily's interest in <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>. The friendship finally ended following the incident that Harry had briefly witnessed in his fifth year, in which Snape accidentally insulted Lily. Despite this separation, and Snape's enmity toward Lily's eventual husband James Potter, Snape continued to love Lily on a much deeper and stronger romantic level for the rest of his life.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Snape was next seen going to Dumbledore and desperately begging him to hide the Potters from Lord Voldemort, who was planning on targeting Lily's son to prevent <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">a prophecy</a> from being fulfilled. Snape had been the one who previously revealed said prophecy to Voldemort, not knowing at first that it was referring to Lily and her family. Though he asked Voldemort to spare Lily, Snape still feared for her safety, as he knew that Voldemort could not be relied on to grant this small favour. Snape became a double agent for the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> so that Dumbledore could ensure Lily's protection, employing <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> to hide his duplicity from his master.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Snape felt devastating pain and remorse when Lily was found and murdered. From that point on, he agreed to help Dumbledore protect her son and fight against Lord Voldemort. Snape demanded, however, that his feelings about Lily be kept a secret. Dumbledore complied and never told anyone the real reason why Snape switched sides.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811020304" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt&#39;s_Ring.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811020304" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore wearing Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s Ring.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt&#39;s_Ring.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/49/Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180811020304" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_wearing_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_Ring.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Marvolo Gaunt's ring with a curse that was slowly killing Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's memories then revealed that Severus slowed the spread of the curse afflicted on Dumbledore, after he put Marvolo Gaunt's ring. However, the curse would have ultimately killed Albus within a year. Dumbledore, knowing that Draco Malfoy was ordered by Voldemort to kill him, and expecting the boy will fail, asked Snape to kill himself instead of Draco in order to gain Voldemort's complete trust and learn more of his plans.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end Snape's memories showed Snape's outrage after learning that Harry had to die. Snape ultimately revealed his Patronus, a doe, the same as Lily's, showing he still, after all these years, loved her.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Because of the memories, Harry finally understood where Snape's true allegiances always were. The memories provided Harry with the information he needed to ensure Voldemort's final defeat. He also showed Harry the memory where Albus Dumbledore had told him about Harry himself being a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> (although he did not understand it) because Dumbledore had asked him to pass that along to Harry when the time was right.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-mortem">Post-mortem</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Post-mortem">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Post-mortem"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Severus Snape wasn't yours, Snape was Dumbledore's, Dumbledore's from the moment you started hunting down my mother!... He was Dumbledore's spy from the moment you threatened her, and he's been working against you ever since!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry reveals Snape's true colours during the final duel<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The final duel between <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and Lord Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the final duel between Harry and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>, Harry finally told him that Snape had been, in fact, Dumbledore's man. Harry also revealed that Snape was never the true master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>, because Snape never defeated Dumbledore; the two had arranged his death as he would have died either way. Before Snape killed Dumbledore, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarmed</a> Dumbledore. Therefore, Draco was the true master of the Elder Wand, not Snape. However, Harry had overpowered Draco at Malfoy Manor and taken his wand. Because of the subtleties governing wand ownership discussed by <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a>, Harry was the current master of the Elder Wand. Snape's true loyalties remained hidden due to his skills as an <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumens</a> and the fact his actions were motivated by love, which completely eluded Voldemort.<sup id="cite_ref-DH36_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH36-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Snape's <a href="/wiki/Headmaster_portraits" title="Headmaster portraits">portrait</a> was not automatically put into the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Headmaster&#39;s office">Headmaster's office</a> since he had essentially abandoned his post during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. However, Harry, in one of his acts of showing reconciliation towards Snape, made sure that <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_portrait" title="Severus Snape&#39;s portrait">his portrait</a> was placed there.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> It is possible that Harry gave his corpse a proper burial after the war ended. <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> also published a book about Snape's life, entitled <i><a href="/wiki/Snape:_Scoundrel_or_Saint%3F" title="Snape: Scoundrel or Saint?">Snape: Scoundrel or Saint?</a></i>, sometime after his death.<sup id="cite_ref-bloomsbury-20070730_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bloomsbury-20070730-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> If it is consistent with Skeeter's other works, it is probably riddled with inaccuracies designed to tarnish Snape's reputation.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus Potter</a>, the second son of Harry, and the only one of Harry's children to have inherited Lily's bright green almond-shaped eyes, is named after Snape. When Albus was worried that he may be Sorted into Slytherin, Harry responded that Albus was named after two headmasters, one of whom was a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> and "<i>probably the bravest man I ever knew</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternate_timeline">Alternate timeline</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Alternate timeline">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Alternate timeline"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>By his fourth year at Hogwarts, <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> had learned all about Snape's history and motivations, allowing him to convince an alternate version of Snape — in a timeline where Voldemort won the Battle of Hogwarts and thus ruled wizarding Britain — that he came from a different timeline so that Snape could help Scorpius meet the local resistance and undo what he had unwittingly done to the past. This version of Snape correctly guessed that he had died in the struggle against Voldemort in Scorpius' timeline but proceeded to aid him nonetheless. After <a href="/wiki/Banishing_Charm" title="Banishing Charm">knocking down</a> <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> to allow <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> to escape, he was attacked by the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, leaving his fate unknown.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span>"<i>...he most likely valued other qualities within himself.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> on why Snape was so poorly groomed<sup id="cite_ref-bloomsbury-20070730_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bloomsbury-20070730-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 158px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20120222145646" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="156" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="SnapeHBP.JPG" data-image-key="SnapeHBP.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20120222145646" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20120222145646" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20120222145646" decoding="async" width="156" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="SnapeHBP.JPG" data-image-key="SnapeHBP.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/SnapeHBP.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20120222145646" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeHBP.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus Snape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus Snape was a thin man with sallow skin, a large, hooked nose and yellow, uneven teeth. He usually dressed in flowing black robes which made him resemble "<i>an overgrown bat</i>". He had shoulder-length, greasy black hair which framed his face in curtains, curling lips and dark, penetrating eyes that resembled tunnels. As a Death Eater, he bore the Dark Mark on his left inner forearm.
</p><p>The younger Snape had a "<i>stringy, pallid look</i>", being "<i>round-shouldered yet angular</i>" and with a "<i>twitchy walk that recalled a spider</i>", as well as "<i>long oily hair that jumped about his face</i>."
</p><p>Snape had a strong, authoritative presence. He spoke in a soft, contained voice most of the time, except during the occasional instances when he lost his temper.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Don't push it. I've heard Snape can turn very nasty.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's infamous temper described by Ronald Weasley<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 234px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027180649" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="232" height="96" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Potion Class.png" data-image-key="Potion_Class.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/232?cb=20131027180649" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027180649" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/232?cb=20131027180649" decoding="async" width="232" height="96" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Potion Class.png" data-image-key="Potion_Class.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/Potion_Class.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/232?cb=20131027180649" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Potion_Class.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">His first potion class with Harry and the rest of the students, where he lecturers Harry in front of the class for "not paying attention" when he was taking notes</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A complicated, withdrawn person, Severus Snape's life was overwhelmed with many complex emotions that he never fully disclosed. At times, Snape could appear cold, cynical, malicious, bitter, and sarcastic. He had a commanding presence that exuded gravitas, authority and control; like <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>, he had the ability to keep a class quiet without effort. He tended to hold grudges and was extremely spiteful toward those whom he disliked. In particular, he disdained <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students, considering them to be arrogant and attention-seeking. Descriptions of his social interactions as a child suggest that he had poor interpersonal skills and that he may have suffered from depression.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20160822105257" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" data-image-key="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20160822105257" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20160822105257" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20160822105257" decoding="async" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" data-image-key="SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20160822105257" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeHarryRonClass.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape's brand of class discipline toward Gryffindors</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape was a repressed, solitary man with no friends. In his early life, he was insecure, vulnerable, and yearned to be part of something better. As a child, the bleak normality of working-class suburbia compounded with his neglectful <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">father</a> inspired in him a contempt for ordinariness. This urgent desire to be a part of something powerful and important was what drew him to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">inner circle</a>. Snape's bitterness and resentment towards the world was exacerbated even more by the relentless bullying he endured in school, causing him to shut himself in even more. Snape was not a prejudiced individual despite the Death Eater beliefs of pure-blood superiority, but was rather against Muggles, presumably because of his sour experience with both his father and Petunia Evans, but held no ill-will towards <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a>. The foundation of him scolding Lily Evans by calling her Mudblood was to not appear weak in front of his fellow Death Eater students than actual supremacist views. He also deeply regretted this as it was what ended his friendship with Lily and defended Hermione Granger when <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> called her Mudblood, his manner of speaking in this instance being uncharacteristically explosive and filled with more emotion than he normally displayed.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Fools who wear their hearts proudly on their sleeves, who cannot control their emotions, who wallow in sad memories and allow themselves to be provoked this easily — weak people, in other words — they stand no chance against his powers!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's opinion on emotionalism and self-control<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141009143617" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape&amp;harry.gif" data-image-key="Snape&amp;harry.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141009143617" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest?cb=20141009143617" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141009143617" decoding="async" width="241" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape&amp;harry.gif" data-image-key="Snape&amp;harry.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Snape%26harry.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20141009143617" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape%26harry.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape threatens Harry after an Occlumency lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He was an intensely private individual who viewed emotional displays as a sign of shameful weakness. As an <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumens</a>, Snape had superb emotional control and was adept at concealing his thoughts and feelings, which allowed him to maintain his cold, collected demeanour. However, he had his limits, and was not incapable of losing his temper, particularly when it came to dealing with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Inevitably, he also became furious when he thought he was being pitied or accused of cowardice.
</p><p>Snape was a formidable sorcerer, displaying consummate skill in many different branches of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>. His extensive knowledge and abilities were rivalled by very few, if any other <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witches and wizards</a> of his age. Snape was also unusually cerebral for a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, possessing a subtle and keenly analytical mind. As a result, Snape was extremely intelligent and calculative, with a mind for strategy and deduction. He was also a profound misanthrope who appeared to have a prominent hatred of almost every child under his tutelage, except of course for <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a>. He valued logic and cunning above magical power.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>After this year, of course, many of you will cease studying with me. I take only the very best into my N.E.W.T. Potions class, which means that some of us will certainly be saying good-bye.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's very high standards as a teacher<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170721221152" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170721221152" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170721221152" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170721221152" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a2/Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170721221152" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-snape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape slapping Ron Weasley over the head with a book for laughing</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a professor, Snape was known for his cavalier and harshly authoritarian attitude towards his teaching. His standards for his classes were much higher than that of the other professors, as he only allowed students with the very best grades to continue into advanced study. As Potions Master, he described it as an art and an exact science, and dismissed the use of incantations and wand waving as "silly and foolish". He developed a loving passion for Dark Arts, originally in the hopes to cover the shame of his heritage, and his interest in it led him to repeatedly apply for the Defence Against the Dark Arts professor post every year, despite being rejected for sixteen years. He knew full well why Dumbledore never granted him the position, as it may be a trigger to bring out his worst side, something he denied to Umbridge's questioning but let in to those of Bellatrix's. When he finally got his wish, Snape taught the course with a loving caress in his voice, far beyond simply respecting the Dark Arts as a dangerous foe, something he did not show in his post as the Potions Master. He also taught this class slightly fairer than he did in Potions, such as lowering his entrance standards and biases for <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T. level</a> classes, allowing more students to enter the advanced studies of his favourite class, and placed students from his own house, such as <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, in detention for failing to do acceptable work the second time around after failing their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> the previous year.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20111111161715" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape&#39;sPatronus.JPG" data-image-key="Snape&#39;sPatronus.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111111161715" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20111111161715" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111111161715" decoding="async" width="251" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape&#39;sPatronus.JPG" data-image-key="Snape&#39;sPatronus.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/Snape%27sPatronus.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20111111161715" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape%27sPatronus.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape showing Dumbledore his true and undying love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ultimately, it was Snape's past and his love for Lily Evans that defined his inner being. His love for Lily Evans became most noticeable by his Patronus; a Doe, just like Lily's. Upon overhearing <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the Prophecy</a>, he immediately informed his then-master of its contents, unaware that this would endanger Lily and her family. It was only after <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">Lily's death</a> that Snape realised the full extent of his actions. He suffered terrible remorse for what he had done and spent the rest of his life in constant danger in order to protect Lily's son.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You are a braver man by far than Igor Karkaroff. You know, I sometimes think we <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sort</a> too soon...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's bravery despite the dangers to his own life<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>In spite of his vindictive demeanour, Severus Snape was an immensely brave man who possessed a deep capacity for <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>. Everything that he did in the latter part of his life was motivated by his devotion to Lily Evans, whom he loved unconditionally. He was one of Dumbledore's most reliable allies and in his role as a double agent, took great personal risk in ensuring Harry's safety from Lord Voldemort. Despite his years of him and Harry barely getting along, if at all, Snape openly criticised Dumbledore after learning he protected Harry all these years just so he could die at the right time due to being a Horcrux, showing he didn't agree with Harry's death even though, at first, he only protected him because of his relationship to Lily. When he informed Dumbledore that he informed Voldemort of the prophecy, Snape begged Dumbledore to hide Harry, Lily, and even James too. This clearly showed that Snape prioritised Lily's happiness above all else, even if it meant her being with a man he hated for most of his life. 
</p><p>Despite his coldness towards all but Lily, Snape nevertheless proved capable of genuinely caring for others apart from Lily and Harry. He showed that despite his mistreatment of them, he cared considerably for the students of Hogwarts, risking his façade for them by secretly doing everything he can to make sure they stayed out of harms way and at one point being genuinely concerned when a student was taken to the Chamber of Secrets. Additionally, Snape was also genuinely saddened by the death of Rowan Khanna, his face just as mournful as the rest of the other House Heads, and if Rowan were in Slytherin, Snape even went as far as to plead with Merula to stop being angry and comfort them with the prospect of standing together in the face of crisis. While he initially resented Dumbledore for his lack of intervention on his torturous bullying by the Marauders, it seemed the time he spent allying with Dumbledore had made him grow to genuinely as well as greatly respect and even care for him, as shown by how he was clearly shocked into being silent for a long time after Dumbledore asked Snape to kill him, clearly indicated that killing Dumbledore was hard for him to do and tried to make him have Draco kill him instead of having Snape do it. Even after learning of how Dumbledore had wanted Harry to die so Voldemort can be defeated, when preparing to kill Dumbledore, his face was described as being genuinely hateful and disgusted of what he was about to do.
</p><p>Despite Snape's normally calm and controlled exterior and guarded body language, he was in possession of an extraordinarily explosive and almost psychotic temper. This was rarely seen, but an extreme display of rage was most prominently witnessed after Snape killed Dumbledore and was confronted outside of Hagrid's burning house near the edge of the school grounds. The event that triggered this unhinged manifestation of Snape's unrestrained wrath was Harry's accusation of Snape being a coward for killing Dumbledore.
</p><p>Due to the many years of being bullied by Harry's father, and with a need to both vent his immense stress and maintain his cover as a loyal <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, Snape unleashed a terrifying mix of both his emotions and magic in his duel with Harry, taking great pleasure in torturing and punishing the son of his enemy. Unlike in the past where he spoke quietly in his anger, Snape in this instance was screaming and letting so much out, as well as confessing his identity of the Half-Blood Prince to Harry who had attempted to use one of Snape's own invented spells against him. This battle showed Snape's repressed rage in its horrific glory and power. Suffice it to say, Severus Snape was not a man who it was wise to provoke, lest one incur his almost elemental wrath and magical power.  
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140619155902" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Silver Doe Patronus.gif" data-image-key="Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140619155902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140619155902" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140619155902" decoding="async" width="240" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Silver Doe Patronus.gif" data-image-key="Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ee/Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140619155902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Silver_Doe_Patronus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus Snape's corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> (the form of a doe)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Snape knew more curses when he arrived at Hogwarts than half the kids in seventh year.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's proficiency for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Severus Snape was an extremely powerful and skilled <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, showing proficient talent and great knowledge in many different areas of magic. He had an encyclopaedic knowledge and proficiency in potions, was incredibly talented in <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, and was also the only <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> capable of producing a Patronus.
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">Magical</a> mastery</b>: Even at a young age, Severus was a gifted wizard, having knowledge of deep secrets of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> that he would usually relay to his crush, <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter" title="Lily Potter">Lily Potter</a>. In addition, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, a known rival of his, claimed that Severus knew more about the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> than half of the seventh year's at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, which speaks for his seemingly encyclopaedic knowledge of magic. He was proficient in creating many useful spells used by the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and even his rivals. He was also proficient in altering the formula for potions, resulting in an easier and more efficient way to produce them, which enhanced <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s proficiency in Potions to the point of easily surpassing even the results of Hermione Granger. His magical prowess was so great as a teenager that his bully and rival, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> would never have taken him on in a one on one fight unless he was backed up by his three other <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">talented friends</a>. As an adult, Snape had became an incredibly powerful and skilled wizard and acknowledged by his fellow professors and <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> for his great prowess. He proved capable of effortlessly defeating the likes of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and also holding his own against the extremely powerful witch <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, who was capable of surviving a duel with Voldemort himself.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">Love</a></b>: Severus was one of the only people in Voldemort's inner circle who was capable of feeling unconditional love. He fell deeply in love with <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> as a child and maintained his devotion to her until his death. Despite their differences in beliefs about many things, Severus felt nothing but absolute love for Lily even though she never extended her reciprocity beyond friendship. Snape was devastated by Lily's death and expressed suicidal desires. However, so great was his love, he forced his way past them and spent seventeen years in constant danger in order to protect Lily's son and ensure that her sacrifice was not in vain. Indeed, Snape's <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> was a doe, just like Lily's, showing that his love for her was far stronger than his loyalty to Lord Voldemort. Due to this, Snape was the only <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> who was able to cast a Patronus. Furthermore, his insight into the nature of love was evident when teaching <a href="/wiki/Love_Potion" class="mw-redirect" title="Love Potion">Love Potions</a>, as he was able to distinguish between the obsessive love caused by love potions and the genuine, unconditional love that most people felt for each other.<sup id="cite_ref-HM5V_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HM5V-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Snape had directed his wand straight at James; there was a flash of light and a gash appeared on the side of James’s face, spattering his robes with blood.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape cursing James Potter with <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Severus had a passion for the Dark Arts from a young age, and was especially talented with <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a>, or so some believed. According to Sirius Black, Snape was "<i>up to his eyeballs in the Dark Arts</i>" when he was at school. However, they had an age old rivalry which could have influenced Sirius's words. When he was still a student, Snape was already talented enough that he was capable of creating new dark spells, as most of the spells he created were curses, <a href="/wiki/Hex" title="Hex">hexes</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxes</a>. As an adult at least, Snape was capable of performing the <a href="/wiki/Killing_Curse" title="Killing Curse">Killing Curse</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a> that required a considerable level of magical skill, using the curse to kill Dumbledore on his orders.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Excuse me. But I believe I am the Potions master at this school.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape to <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Severus was extremely adept in the art of potion-making and worked as the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> at Hogwarts for about fifteen years. His prowess at potion-making extended beyond simple execution from formally documented recipes accepted and followed by the general public. When he was still only a student, he would alter official instructions with his own variations, which usually resulted in quicker and more efficient results. He was capable of brewing highly complicated potions such as <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wolfsbane_Potion" title="Wolfsbane Potion">Wolfsbane Potion</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a>. Snape was also able to identify <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> by smell and produce fake Veritaserum that seemed real enough to fool Dolores Umbridge (though Umbridge was not portrayed as being particularly intelligent with practicality). In addition, Snape used an <a href="/wiki/Thick_golden_potion" title="Thick golden potion">unidentified golden potion</a> to help slow a <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">curse</a> that was slowly killing Dumbledore.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Your defences must therefore be as flexible and inventive as the arts you seek to undo.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape teaching <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth year</a> Defence Against the Dark Arts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Though Snape had a zest for dark magic, he possessed outstanding knowledge and abilities in protecting from it. His encyclopaedic understanding of the dark arts may have contributed to this. Snape taught the class at N.E.W.T level to such an effect that even Harry Potter could not help but be enchanted by his knowledge. Snape effectively "assisted" the 1992 duelling club, and understood the need for students handling pragmatism as well as theory in the subject. Snape's speciality in DADA was particularly in the area of counter-curses. In fact, his abilities in countering curses were so great that he was able to temporarily save Dumbledore (himself an expert on the subject) with wand enhanced incantations and a <a href="/wiki/Thick_golden_potion" title="Thick golden potion">potion</a> simultaneously from a "<i>curse of extraordinary power</i>", Dumbledore noted that he was only able to (temporarily) survive due to Snape's expertise. He was also able to prevent the curse that Katie Bell was inflicted with when she touched the necklace on Borgin and Burkes from spreading any further, saving her life. Snape had also developed effective counter curses for his own <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charms</a>, such as the magic he used to heal Draco from the effects of <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>We are going to see how well you resist. I have been told that you have already shown aptitude at resisting the Imperius Curse.... You will find that similar powers are needed for this.... Brace yourself, now.... Legilimens!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape using the <a href="/wiki/Legilimency_Spell" title="Legilimency Spell">Legilimency Spell</a> on Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a></b>: Snape's unerring ability to conceal his thoughts and feelings from external penetration proved to be crucial for him. His skills in Occlumency was so great that for seventeen years, he managed to hide facts from <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> such as his remorse for Lily Evans's death and his secret alliance with Albus Dumbledore; it was his mastery of hiding his mind that made both sides distrust him. Snape was also very skilled at Legilimency; Harry Potter often felt as if Snape had the ability to read minds even before learning what the art was. Snape used Legilimency on Harry constantly, while attempting to teach him Occlumency in their private lessons and later used it to effortlessly deflect Harry's spells and curses. Despite his skill in Legilimency he was may have been unable to read <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>'s thoughts when the latter was a relatively inexperienced Occlumens (though Draco may have only believed that he was able to block Snape). Since Voldemort was considered history's greatest legilimens and was unable to ever read Snape's mind, despite being in the same room with him on many occasions, Snape could be history's greatest occlumens, with the possible exception of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gellert_Grindelwald" title="Gellert Grindelwald">Gellert Grindelwald</a>, both of whom proved able to also deflect Voldemort's Legilimency. Considering how Voldemort would have detected Snape resisting penetration, Snape would've had to be careful only to block certain thoughts from him while allowing Voldemort to only see what would reinforce his belief in Snape's loyalty.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>Snape stepped forward, waved his wand, and the snake vanished in a small puff of black smoke.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape performing the <a href="/wiki/Snake-Vanishing_Spell" title="Snake-Vanishing Spell">Snake-Vanishing Spell</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Severus was highly accomplished with transfiguration, given his proficiency with <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">Conjuration</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vanishment" title="Vanishment">Vanishment</a>, two very difficult and advanced branches of this field. He was talented with the vanishing of physical matter, as shown when he vanished Harry Potter's failed <a href="/wiki/Draught_of_Peace" title="Draught of Peace">Draught of Peace</a> potion in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Vanishing_Spell" title="Vanishing Spell">Vanishing Spell</a><sup id="cite_ref-OOTP12_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP12-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> and when he vanished the <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a> that <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> <a href="/wiki/Snake_Summons_Spell" title="Snake Summons Spell">summoned</a> in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Snake-Vanishing_Spell" title="Snake-Vanishing Spell">Snake-Vanishing Spell</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-COS11_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS11-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> He also successfully conjured ropes with the <a href="/wiki/Incarcerous_Spell" title="Incarcerous Spell">Incarcerous Spell</a> to bind <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA19_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA19-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He also transfigured the whirlwind-shaped fire that McGonagall launched at him shortly before the Battle of Hogwarts into a great black snake.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_61-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>From the tip of his wand burst the silver doe: she landed on the office floor, bounded once across the office and soared out of the window. Dumbledore watched her fly away, and as her silvery glow faded he turned back to Snape, and his eyes were full of tears.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape conjuring a corporeal Patronus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Snape was highly talented in charms as he not only could use basic to advanced charms without fail, such as <a href="/wiki/Levitation" title="Levitation">levitation</a>, <a href="/wiki/Disarming_charm" class="mw-redirect" title="Disarming charm">disarming</a>, <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">summoning</a>, <a href="/wiki/Banishing_Charm" title="Banishing Charm">banishing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Locking_Spell" title="Locking Spell">locking doors</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mending_Charm" title="Mending Charm">repairing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wand-Lighting_Charm" title="Wand-Lighting Charm">illuminating</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">igniting</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water-Making_Spell" title="Water-Making Spell">creating water</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">shielding</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunning</a>, but he was even able to cast the incredibly difficult <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>, conjuring a corporeal doe Patronus. He was also able to <a href="/wiki/Blackboard_Writing_Spell" title="Blackboard Writing Spell">write instructions on a blackboard</a> with a single flick of his wand.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>With a tingle of horror, Harry saw in the distance a huge, <a href="/wiki/Bat" title="Bat">bat</a>-like shape flying through the darkness towards the perimeter wall.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape flying without support<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Snape was a very capable flyer on a <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a>, as during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, he was not blasted off his broom and knowledgeable enough in the rules of <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> to take over the position of referee at least once. However, in one of Snape's memories, Lily was laughing as he attempted to mount a bucking broomstick, so perhaps he was not always a good flyer. Later on, Severus was also capable of <a href="/wiki/Unsupported_flight" title="Unsupported flight">Unsupported flight</a>. The only other known wizard that was able to do this was Lord Voldemort himself (who is likely to have passed down this skill to Snape personally). In 1997, he used this skill to escape from Hogwarts after his duel with Minerva McGonagall.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 156px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104725" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="154" height="233" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" data-image-key="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20160819104725" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104725" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20160819104725" decoding="async" width="154" height="233" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" data-image-key="SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0d/SnapeDuelingClub.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/154?cb=20160819104725" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:SnapeDuelingClub.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape in a duelling demonstration during the first meeting of the <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Professor McGonagall moved faster than Harry could have believed: her wand slashed through the air and for a split second Harry thought that Snape must crumple, unconscious, but the swiftness of his Shield Charm was such that McGonagall was thrown off balance.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape duelling Minerva McGonagall<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Although he rarely engaged in duels, Snape was shown to be a highly capable duellist. During his days as a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> he likely had to fight against <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">aurors</a> and members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. He was able to hold his own against the extremely powerful <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> (who was capable of duelling Voldemort along with Kingsley and Slughorn) during their brief duel, before she forced him to hide behind a shield of armour. He then fled when <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a> and <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> arrived to assist He assisted in a duelling club in 1992 with <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, effortlessly defeating him with a single spell, though, as Lockhart was an unskilled wizard, this was not such a great achievement. Snape also easily overwhelmed <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during his escape from the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and defeated him without much effort, using <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimency</a> to read Harry's attempted moves and countered them all before they could be cast. Severus participated in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, joining the Death Eaters's side (though secretly attempted to protect the Order), and survived unharmed. Contrary to the vicious duelling styles of other Death Eaters, Snape preferred using defensive spells and only used aggressive magic when facing a weak opponent, such as Lockhart, or when his foe grew frustrated and started making mistakes. Snape was never known to battle a Death Eater or ally to Voldemort (which would've blown his cover) but no Death Eater ever dared raise a wand against him (even the notoriously powerful <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>) and showed fear towards him, indicating they must have seen him display remarkable duelling skills.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>You dare use my own spells against me, Potter? It was I who invented them — I, the Half Blood Prince! And you’d turn my inventions on me, like your filthy father, would you? I don’t think so...no!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape revealing Harry Potter his talent with spell invention<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Spell_creation" title="Spell creation">Spell creation</a></b>: As a student at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Severus was very inventive with new <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a>. Some of the spells he created were <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Langlock" title="Langlock">Langlock</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Muffliato_Charm" title="Muffliato Charm">Muffliato</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Levicorpus" title="Levicorpus">Levicorpus</a></i> and its <a href="/wiki/Counter-jinx" title="Counter-jinx">Counter-jinx</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Liberacorpus" title="Liberacorpus">Liberacorpus</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP28_25-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP28-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> The last two somehow became common knowledge around the school. It is unknown what thoughts and techniques Snape put into his creations.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>BANG! Thin, snakelike cords brust from the end of Snape's wand and twisted themselves around Lupin's mouth, wrists, and ankles</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjures</a> ropes non-verbally<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Wandless" title="Wandless">Wandless</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">nonverbal</a> magic</b>: Snape was highly skilled at using non-verbal spells, from the most basic uses (such as instruction-writing on blackboards and cleanups) to the most advanced (such as combat curses). Snape was also skilled at performing wandless magic, such as rope conjuring, counter-jinxing and memory extraction. (Although memory extraction does not require explicitly the use of a wand, relying instead on direct eye contact, conjuring and counter-jinxing are more often depicted to take place with the help of a wand.)</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Alchemy" title="Alchemy">Alchemy</a></b>: Intimately connected with <a href="/wiki/Potions" class="mw-redirect" title="Potions">potion-making</a> among other things, Snape had great respect for the field of alchemy, believing it was as much about gaining intellectual wealth as the physical one. Deeming it more advanced than his <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">usual lessons</a>, to the point where he initially asked <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> if the latter was joking when they asked whether he would be willing to teach alchemy to themselves and the visiting <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons</a> <a href="/wiki/Aur%C3%A9lie_Dumont" title="Aurélie Dumont">student</a>, insisting that he would only ever consider giving lessons on the subject to a select few of his very best students, such as <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a>.
