Displaying a fair amount of knowledge on the topic, he was able to host a private lesson and give <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>, <a href="/wiki/Penny_Haywood" title="Penny Haywood">Penny Haywood</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aur%C3%A9lie_Dumont" title="Aurélie Dumont">Aurélie Dumont</a> a lecture on the philosophy, history and teachings of the subject, as well as <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">its objectives</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>He knelt over Malfoy, drew his wand, and traced it over the deep wounds Harry’s curse had made, muttering an incantation that sounded almost like song. The flow of blood seemed to ease; Snape wiped the residue from Malfoy’s face and repeated his spell. Now the wounds seemed to be knitting.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape healing a wounded Draco Malfoy<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Healing_magic" title="Healing magic">Healing magic</a></b>: Snape was also very skilled with healing magic, as he reduced the effects of the <a href="/wiki/Curse_on_Marvolo_Gaunt%27s_ring" title="Curse on Marvolo Gaunt&#39;s ring">Curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring</a> on <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> which allowed him to survive for at least a year and saved <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a>'s life by preventing any further spread of the <a href="/wiki/Opal_Necklace" title="Opal Necklace">cursed necklace</a> in her body.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> He also healed <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>'s wounds with <i><a href="/wiki/Vulnera_Sanentur" title="Vulnera Sanentur">Vulnera Sanentur</a>,</i> a <a href="/wiki/Healing_spell" title="Healing spell">healing spell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">counter-curse</a>, after Harry Potter recklessly used the <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> curse on him and seriously injured him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP24_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP24-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> His knowledge in healing was such that Dumbledore once quoted to Harry that Snape was more experienced in healing against Dark magic than <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a> was. He also successfully brewed the <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draught</a> in the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992–1993 school year</a>, which cured all the victims of <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrification</a> that year.<sup id="cite_ref-COS9_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS9-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a></b>: Like most accomplished adult wizards, Snape could apparate successfully at will. He disapparated away from Hogwarts after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a> from beyond the Hogwarts gates.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP28_25-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP28-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Intellectual giftedness</b>: Snape's logic and deductive reasoning skills were such that he helped protect the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> by creating an obstacle, which was based on logic rather than magical skill. According to <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, many powerful wizards have a blind spot in regards to logic.<sup id="cite_ref-PS16_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS16-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Teaching skills</b>: Despite his unpleasant nature and strained relationship with many of the Hogwarts students outside <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, Snape was nevertheless a relatively effective teacher as the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> and was one of the few teachers at Hogwarts who could keep a class quiet with minimal effort, with some students like <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> able to achieve <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a> under his teaching, despite Snape only allowing students with top grades to do Potions in the NEWT level. His teaching skills were also effective enough for him to be respected by most of the other professors until he killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>, pass <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>'s inspection of him and for <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> to make him <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a> of Hogwarts. Additionally, while <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> did not learn much from Snape due to their mutual dislike of each other, the instructions Snape wrote in his <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">Copy of Advanced Potion-Making</a> were effective enough to make Harry improve his own performance in Potions in his sixth year, suggesting that Snape would have been more respected as a teacher if he was less unpleasant and used these instructions more.</li>
<li><b>Acting skills</b>: Snape was an extremely adept actor, as he flawlessly succeeded in hiding his true allegiance to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, even able to fool <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> himself completely to the point of the latter having complete trust in him to such an extent that after he killed Dumbledore, Voldemort was fully willing to make him Hogwart's <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>. Snape's skill in acting allowed him to keep his motives dubious in the eyes of both friend and ally alike. This makes Snape likely the most accomplished actor and spy in wizarding history.</li>
<li><b>Poetry</b>: A skill that Snape possessed but did not make very much mention or display of, Snape was capable of fluidly crafting his words in a way that could often befuddle the reader. His only known composition was the logic puzzle that he used as part of his defences of the Philosopher's Stone. Since this poem showed Snape's logical thinking, it was obviously one of his own creation. Snape's other possible works, if they exist, remain unknown.</li>
<li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: Snape, despite his personal demons, possessed immense willpower and bravery, being a respected hero of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> and having great respect from both <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> (the latter of whom would go so far as to declare Snape to be "the bravest man [he] ever knew"). Hence, despite his great love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_Potter" title="Lily Potter">Lily Potter</a> and being aware of her intense disapproval for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, Snape refused to relinquish his interest for the practice nor abandon the approval of his <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> friends for her. Later, while guilt-ridden and devastated, feeling personally responsible for Lily's death, Snape refused to succumb to despair and instead dedicated himself to honouring Lily in death by working closely with Dumbledore to protect Harry and ensure that her sacrifice was not in vain. As such, despite the extremely dangerous and seemingly impossible task of bringing down the most powerful <a href="/wiki/Dark_wizard" class="mw-redirect" title="Dark wizard">Dark wizard</a> of all time, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Snape refused to back down from it and resolved to faithfully execute Dumbledore's many complex and intricate plans to bring down the Dark Lord, with him valiantly working as an undercover agent for the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> for sixteen years and steadfastly spying on the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, with this ultimately ensuring Voldemort's defeat at the hands of Harry. Snape's willpower and determination also allowed him to persistently apply for the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> post for fifteen years (despite Dumbledore repeatedly refusing him the job) and to completely master the notably difficult skills of <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Non-verbal_magic" class="mw-redirect" title="Non-verbal magic">non-verbal magic</a>, both of which required high amounts of mental strength. Moreover, in an alternate timeline, Snape was willing to sacrifice himself to defeat Voldemort and save the world once again, by distracting a swarm of <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, thereby giving <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> the necessary opening to restore the timeline again.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Parents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Parents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Lily Evans</b>: "<i>Doesn't your <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">dad</a> like magic?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>He doesn't like anything, much.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Severus regarding his father's horrible personality<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Snape never regarded the place where he grew up as a home. Rather like <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> and Harry, <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> was his real home. It is likely that he suffered neglect as a child. His parents seem to have had a dysfunctional, even abusive relationship. This troubled, lonely childhood is strongly suggested to have accounted for his severe demeanour, depression, sadness, bitterness, and bouts of rage, as seen later in his life. 
</p><p>Despite having a father who disliked the wizarding community, Snape was quite skilled with magic before he even received his Hogwarts letter. Sirius Black would later remark that, when they first arrived at school, Snape knew more curses than many of the seventh-year students. It does seem that he had a slightly better relationship with his witch mother. During his school years, he nicknamed himself the "Half Blood Prince". In addition, it is quite likely <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen</a> gave her son most, if not all of his school things. His <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">sixth-year Potions book</a> was, according to Harry, at least fifty years old. 
</p><p>Since at least 1996, Snape was staying in his family's home during the summers between school years. It is unknown what happened to his parents. As he was only thirty-six years old in 1996, his parents may well have been alive, but moved away and left the house to him. His salary as a Hogwarts professor probably made it possible for him to afford other lodging during summers, but his childhood memories of Lily may have stopped him from abandoning the house. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lily_Evans">Lily Evans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lily Evans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Lily Evans"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Look...at....me....</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape wanting one last glimpse of Lily's eyes<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 163px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="161" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140712171247" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140712171247" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140712171247" decoding="async" width="161" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lily Potter1.jpg" data-image-key="Lily_Potter1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Lily_Potter1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/161?cb=20140712171247" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lily_Potter1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lily Evans, his once best friend and love of his life</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's friendship with <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> was probably the only thing that truly brought joy to his life. He first met Lily at a very young age, recognising her as a witch one day as she and her sister <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia</a> played in the park near his house; she had flown off the swings and made a flower grow from a sprout. Longing to escape his humiliating home life, Snape immediately sought to make her his friend. Despite the fact that Lily came from a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> family, he never truly saw her as being one of them because he was so smitten with her. 
</p><p>They spend time talking about magic and the wizarding world. Lily even asked if being Muggle-born matter in the Wizarding world, which Snape responded that it did not matter at all. In 1971, the two of them were accepted into <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> and continued a close friendship up until around their fifth year, despite being Sorted into different houses. Snape was very disappointed that they were not in the same house and forlorn because of it.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>James Potter</b>: "<i>There you go, you’re lucky Evans was here, Snivellus —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>I don’t need help from filthy little Mudbloods like her!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Lily Evans</b>: "<i>Fine. I won’t bother in future. And I’d wash your pants if I were you, Snivellus.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; The unpleasant end of Snape and Lily's friendship<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>During this time, Snape began hanging out with people who embraced Dark Magic and <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pure-blood supremacy</a>, which put a huge strain on their friendship. Lily was offended by many of the views that Snape was beginning to adopt and disliked the qualities that his new classmates were bringing out in him. Given time over again, Snape would never have done many of the things he did, but at the time he did not truly understand her aversion. He was so insecure and blinded by his attraction to the Dark side that he imagined she would find it impressive if he became a real Death Eater. Ironically, Lily might have grown to love Snape romantically (she certainly loved him as a friend) if he had not loved Dark Magic so much, and been drawn to such loathsome people and acts. When Snape called Lily a "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" in a moment of humiliation, it was the last straw for Lily. When she later asked him if he still intended to become a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> and he did not deny it, she severed all ties with him, despite Snape's profuse apologies.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest?cb=20111026150555" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" data-image-key="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111026150555" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest?cb=20111026150555" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111026150555" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" data-image-key="Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/99/Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111026150555" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Vlcsnap-2011-10-26-11h05m22s7.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lily and Severus talking by the riverside</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Snape overheard <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the Prophecy</a>, he immediately relayed its contents to the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Dark Lord</a>, not knowing that it would have anything to do with Lily. Upon discovering that Lord Voldemort was planning on targeting the Potter family, Snape pleaded with him to spare Lily in exchange for her husband and son. He later appealed to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, asking him to do everything in his power to protect Lily and the rest of her family, if he had to.
</p><p>Snape was devastated by Lily's death, to the point of sinking into a depression that seemingly lasted the rest of his life. However, at Dumbledore's behest, he became committed to protecting her son Harry and assisting him in defeating the Dark Lord. Snape never spoke of Lily to anyone again, except for Dumbledore. This was likely due to heartbreak and worry that mention of her might make others suspicious. Even though he constantly slandered James to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Lily's son's</a> face, he alienated Lily from these attacks entirely, possibly due to his inability to ever insult her again. Indeed, Snape's Patronus was a doe, just like Lily's, because he loved her throughout his entire life. As Snape died, he asked Harry to look into his eyes; his last wish in his final moments was to die looking into the same green eyes that reminded him so much of Lily. 
</p><p>As a result of Snape's sacrifice of his own life, Lily's son Harry would name <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">her second grandson</a> after Snape. Coincidentally, said grandson would inherit Lily's green eyes. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Marauders">The Marauders</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Marauders">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: The Marauders"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Snape being bullied by the Marauders"><b>James Potter</b>: "<i>How’d the exam go, Snivelly?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>I was watching him, his nose was touching the parchment. There’ll be great grease marks all over it, they won’t be able to read a word.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>You — wait. You — wait....</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>Wait for what? What’re you going to do, Snivelly, wipe your nose on us?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape being bullied by the Marauders<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080414050923" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="186" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Marauders 1997.jpg" data-image-key="Marauders_1997.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20080414050923" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080414050923" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20080414050923" decoding="async" width="235" height="186" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Marauders 1997.jpg" data-image-key="Marauders_1997.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Marauders_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20080414050923" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Marauders_1997.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, his school bullies and enemies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Marauders were a group of four <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> boys, with whom Severus began a relationship of enmity and hatred throughout their school years. The group consisted of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>. Severus and the first two Marauders detested each other almost instantly upon meeting for the first time in a compartment on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. Throughout their times at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, James and his friends (except for Lupin) bullied Snape ceaselessly, Pettigrew only did it though because James and Sirius did it. Lupin did not encourage the harassment, but he did not try to stop them, either. Snape, in turn, never lost an opportunity to get one up on them whenever possible. 
</p><p>However, James Potter ended up saving his life when Sirius told Snape how to get into the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. Snape caught a glimpse of Lupin transforming into a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> before James pulled him back through the tunnel. Snape did not think James was acting nobly. Rather, he saw it as being more of a self-serving act in order to avoid him and the rest of the Marauders being expelled from Hogwarts, and the incident only made him resent James more than ever. He also came to resent Lupin, believing that he had been in on Sirius's prank. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111027074415" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="165" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" data-image-key="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20111027074415" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111027074415" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20111027074415" decoding="async" width="235" height="165" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" data-image-key="MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20111027074415" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:MaraudersPickingOnSnape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Marauders bullying Snape during their time at Hogwarts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>Well, Snape was a special case. I mean, he never lost an opportunity to curse James so you couldn't really expect James to take that lying down, could you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>And my mum was </i>OK<i> with that?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>She didn't know too much about it, to tell you the truth, I mean, James didn't take Snape on dates with her and jinx him in front of her, did he?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Lupin, Harry, and Sirius Black discussing Snape's interactions with Harry's parents during their seventh year<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>During their seventh year at Hogwarts, Lily and James began dating, which probably fuelled Snape's hatred of him even more. James always suspected that Snape had deeper feelings for Lily, which factored strongly into his behaviour towards him. Snape's continued bitterness toward the Marauders, even into adulthood, became apparent in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, when Remus Lupin was given the position of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor at Hogwarts, despite Snape and Dumbledore both knowing that he was a werewolf.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>I’ve told the headmaster again and again that you’re helping your old friend Black into the castle, Lupin, and here’s the proof. Not even I dreamed you would have the nerve to use this old place as your hideout —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>Severus, you’re making a mistake. You haven’t heard everything — I can explain — Sirius is not here to kill Harry —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Two more for Azkaban tonight. I shall be interested to see how Dumbledore takes this... He was quite convinced you were harmless, you know, Lupin... a tame werewolf —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape confronting Sirius Black and Remus Lupin in the Shrieking Shack<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>During the time that Harry Potter attended the school, Snape delighted in comparing Harry to his father and telling him that he was not the great man he liked to believe he was. Although Snape's descriptions of James' teenage self were accurate, Snape purposefully omitted even vague descriptions of the noble person James became. Snape mostly felt bitterness and resentment towards Remus Lupin and took to dropping hints about his being a werewolf in the hopes that the students would catch on. However, it should be noted that, despite Snape's strained relationship with the Marauders, he dutifully concocted potions for Remus Lupin during his tenure at Hogwarts and attempted to save his life during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Flight From Little Whinging</a>. Lupin was the only one of the Marauders who could interact with Snape at least on a perfunctory level when they were adults. Lupin, like everyone, believed Snape an evil, cowardly servant of Voldemort's after Snape killed Albus Dumbledore, and died before learning the truth. 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111108153715" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape Sirius.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_Sirius.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20111108153715" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111108153715" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20111108153715" decoding="async" width="245" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape Sirius.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_Sirius.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Snape_Sirius.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20111108153715" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_Sirius.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape confronts Sirius Black at the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>I’ve warned you, Snivellus I don’t care if Dumbledore thinks you’ve reformed, I know better —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Oh, but why don’t you tell him so? Or are you afraid he might not take the advice of a man who has been hiding inside his mother’s house for six months very seriously?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape and Sirus arguing<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Snape held an especially strong enmity towards Sirius. Although Snape's hatred towards Sirius for the humiliation he put him under alongside James in their Hogwarts years was already great, the fact that Sirius apparently was the Marauder who betrayed Lily to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> made him hate Sirius even more than he did with James. He was eager to be the one to hand Sirius over to receive the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> after he <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes#1993" title="Azkaban escapes">broke out</a> of <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and was furious when he managed to escape yet again. After Sirius's innocence was proven, however, Dumbledore insisted that the two of them shake hands and ally together against Voldemort. Nevertheless, they remained barely capable of civilly conversing, as both of them still resented each other and Snape, in particular, taunted him about his uselessness to the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a> while confined to <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">his mother's house</a>, which escalated in Sirius nearly challenging Snape to a duel, which Snape was eager to and would have gladly accepted had the Weasleys not barged in. However, Sirius himself admitted he felt ashamed of his previous treatment and did not at all enjoy the reminder of the reason for Snape being humiliated due to Sirius being bored in their fifth year. Snape also, even if begrudgingly, accepted that they were fighting for the same side and was quick to check if Sirius was in fact safe after Harry reported to him he saw Sirius tortured by Voldemort and in the Ministry to be forced to retrieve the object.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Well, Wormtail’s here, but we’re not counting vermin, are we? As you have clearly realised, Wormtail, we have guests.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape bullying Wormtail in his home<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Although Snape's relationship with Pettigrew in their school years was already hostile, upon knowing he was the Marauder who truly betrayed Lily, he most likely became the Marauder Snape resented the most. Although forced to keep his dislike as best as he could due to his job as a double-agent for Dumbledore, Snape seized his chance to torment Pettigrew when the Dark Lord later assigned Pettigrew to work as his assistant, treating him like a slave, forcing him to clean his house and serve food to his guests, clearly intent on making sure that Pettigrew would not experience any comfortableness while under his command. Snape also seemed to enjoy threatening Pettigrew by telling Voldemort that he desired more dangerous assignments whenever he would protest his position as Snape's servant.
</p><p>In an ironic twist, despite their mutual antipathy, James' <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">second grandson</a> would be named after Snape years after the deaths of Snape and the Marauders.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>He is his father all over again.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's assessment of Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" decoding="async" width="165" height="220" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20140603201724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his former student and the person he sought to protect</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>From the day Harry set foot in Hogwarts, he and Snape loathed each other. Despite the fact that Snape was committed to honouring <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a>'s sacrifice, he could not bring himself to judge the boy objectively because of his connection to <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, who bullied him in his school days. Indeed, Snape was filled with nothing but contempt and bitterness towards Harry, who simultaneously reminded him of both Lily and James. Harry served as living proof of the fact that Lily had given her <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> to someone else, and Snape wasted no time in comparing him continually with his father.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Ah, yes, Harry Potter. Our new — celebrity.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape insulting Harry Potter in his first lesson with him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>During Harry's time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Snape treated Harry viciously, both in class and out. He frequently derided the boy's abilities, bullied him in class, and punished him whenever possible. He was also resentful and even somewhat envious of Harry's popularity, which he also equated with Harry's father. Although Snape threatened to have Harry expelled more than once, he never attempted to follow through — presumably because it would have led to Harry losing the protection surrounding him. However, never did he forget that Harry was also Lily's child, and much beyond bureaucratic rules, this led him to put the boy's safety in the most critical situation. When he learned that <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> had intended for Harry to die all along, Severus remained horrified, seeing it as a calculated betrayal to Lily's memory.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>You might be labouring under the delusion that the entire wizarding world is impressed with you, but I don’t care how many times your picture appears in the papers. To me, Potter, you are nothing but a nasty little boy who considers rules to be beneath him.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape belittling Harry Potter during a fourth year Potions lesson<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>When Harry helped <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> escape, their relationship went under further strain, since Snape believed at that time that Sirius betrayed Lily to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> whereas Harry had learned of his innocence, although Snape continued to put Harry's safety first. During the brief period in which Snape gave private <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> lessons, Snape relished in forcing Harry to relive his worst memories. During the early years, Harry associated Snape with his abusive and bullying ways but when Sirius died, Harry took a savage pleasure in blaming Snape for having taunted Sirius about being useless, causing him to leave his hiding place and join the battle. 
</p><p>Though Snape came to the aid of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a> as swiftly as possible, Harry blamed Snape mainly to ease his own guilty conscience about the entire incident. However, this was nothing in comparison to the retroactive rage Harry felt upon finding out that Snape was the one who relayed <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the Prophecy</a> to Lord Voldemort, causing him to hunt down Harry and his family. When he later killed Dumbledore, the hatred between them was sealed almost as personally as between Harry and Voldemort.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 245px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122215347" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="243" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" data-image-key="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20141122215347" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122215347" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20141122215347" decoding="async" width="243" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" data-image-key="Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/243?cb=20141122215347" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape-s-last-minutes-severus-snape-27845931-640-472.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape looks into Harry's eyes as he dies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As he lay dying, Snape told Harry to look at him and died looking into Lily's eyes. Following this, Harry was given access to all of Snape's concealed memories, which brought the former teacher's true intentions and more human side to light. When Harry discovered the love Snape had for his mother and the constant danger he put himself in to ensure his safety, his opinion of him changed completely.
</p><p>By adulthood, all of Harry's hatred of Snape seems to have vanished and it looks as though he had never harboured it at all. This can be seen through his request that a <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_portrait" title="Severus Snape&#39;s portrait">portrait of Snape</a> be hung in the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Headmaster&#39;s office">Headmaster's office</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, which was not done immediately after Snape's death since he had abandoned his post. Furthermore, Harry gave his youngest son the name "Albus Severus", and told him that his Slytherin namesake was "<i>the bravest man I ever knew</i>."
</p><p>Another aspect of Snape's highly visible, almost cartoonish mistreatment of Harry is that he knew all his actions might one day be reported to Voldemort by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> spies. He did nothing that would create the image of real sympathy or loyalty to Potter or any of Voldemort's former adversaries, only curt professionalism towards his colleagues, obedience but not true loyalty to Dumbledore, and utter hatred for Harry. His need to behave this way was redoubled when it became clear Voldemort could use legilimency to read Harry's mind, and in doing so view any action by Snape in view of Harry. 
</p><p>Ironically, the two shared many similarities that neither of them was aware of. Both were <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> wizards who grew up among <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>. Both of their Muggle caretakers were cruel to them (Snape's father was implied to be abusive to Snape and his mother, while the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a> were neglectful towards Harry). Both Snape and Harry's childhoods involved <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Evans</a> (Snape was friends with Petunia's sister Lily, while Harry was Petunia's nephew and was raised (albeit reluctantly and abusively) by her). Both grew up wearing secondhand clothes (however, Snape was likely forced to wear them due to his family's poverty, while Harry's relatives simply refused to afford any major expenses on him). In addition, the two grew up virtually friendless until attending Hogwarts (Snape due to his unstable family life and secondhand clothes, Harry due to his relatives isolating him). 
</p><p>Upon entering Hogwarts, Snape and Harry were bullied mercilessly, in Snape's case, by the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a> (who were led by James Potter), and Harry by (ironically) Snape himself, <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, among others. Furthermore, both had at least one near-death experience during their Hogwarts: Snape was nearly killed in an abortive prank by the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, while Harry repeatedly had Voldemort attempting to kill him. However, both Snape and Harry had at least one silver gleaming: their genuinely intense and close romantic attraction to a redheaded teenager (Lily Evans and Ginny Weasley, respectively). Of course, while Snape did not marry Lily (who had married James and mothered Harry), Harry himself did marry Ginny (with whom he had a son named <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a>).
</p><p>In the second alternate timeline created by Scorpius Malfoy and Albus Potter, Scorpius revealed to Snape the predicament he had caused among other things. It is founded that Snape was extremely saddened and disappointed in his failure to protect Harry from Voldemort in the final battle, and was also engaged in assisting <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a> in fixing the timeline so Harry was alive and Voldemort defeated. One of the details he revealed after convincing Snape of his tale was that in his timeline that Harry had named his second son after him. This deeply touched Severus, who later told Scorpius to convey to Albus in the original timeline that he is proud that the boy carries his name and legacy, feeling apart of time he will never experience for the greater good of the world. He died without hesitation for the better world that Scorpius sought to restore, knowing his purpose could finally be served. Snape once again died for the legacy of his love, showing the kind of man he was at heart.
</p><p>After the original timeline was restored, Harry visited Cedric Diggory's grave with Albus, describing his son's two namesakes — Dumbledore and Snape — as very much alike, despite their sorting into different houses: <i>"great men, with huge flaws, and you know what - those flaws almost made them greater."</i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron_Weasley_and_Hermione_Granger">Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley and Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>That is the second time you have spoken out of turn, Miss Granger... Five more points from Gryffindor for being an insufferable know-it-all.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>You asked us a question and she knows the answer! Why ask if you don't want to be told?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Detention, Weasley... and if I ever hear you criticise the way I teach a class again, you will be very sorry indeed.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A typical interaction in Snape's classroom<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191008170323" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="222" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20191008170323" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191008170323" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20191008170323" decoding="async" width="165" height="222" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-image-key="The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/17/The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20191008170323" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-trio-Harry-Potter-and-the-chamber-of-secrets-potterhead-29266030-365-400.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron Weasley and Hermione, two Gryffindor students he often disdained</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape criticised <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> whenever possible, most likely because of the fact that they were friends of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> as well as being <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a>. Although Snape seldom found anything wrong with Hermione's work and marked her grades accordingly, he never awarded her <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">house points</a> and sometimes accused her of being an "<i>insufferable know-it-all</i>". Despite this, Snape saved their lives in 1993 when Professor Lupin had transformed into a werewolf at the full moon, and even after they had stopped being his students, continued to assist the three of them in their quest to destroy the seven Horcruxes (without them being any the wiser, of course). 
</p><p>It is unknown how Ron and Hermione reacted to the revelation of Snape's loyalty though as Harry recounted Snape's memories they were described as shocked. There's also no mention of them protesting Harry and Ginny naming their (Ron &amp; Hermione) nephew after Snape, which might indicate they came to forgive and admire him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>I prefer not to put all my secrets in one basket, particularly not a basket that spends so much time dangling on the arm of Lord Voldemort.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Which I do on your orders!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Albus Dumbledore</b>: "<i>And you do it extremely well. Do not think that I underestimate the constant danger in which you place yourself, Severus. To give Voldemort what appears to be valuable information while withholding the essentials is a job I would entrust to nobody but you.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dumbledore and Snape on the latter's espionage<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="223" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="165" height="223" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his former headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's relationship with Dumbledore was one of close, but not indefinite trust. Dumbledore was Snape's headmaster whilst at Hogwarts and was presumably impressed with Snape's academia and abilities. Snape likely felt no real loyalty to Dumbledore as a student and may have resented the latter's failure for stopping the torturous bullying Snape received at the hands of the Marauders. Despite this, he agreed to keep Remus Lupin's lycanthropy a secret when the headmaster ordered him (though likely out of self-serving reasons). Before allying himself with Snape, Dumbledore viewed him with, in his own words, disgust, for the latter's selfishness.
</p><p>After having accidentally put Lily's life in jeopardy by delivering a prophecy to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> (without knowing at the time that it was referring to her son), Snape turned to Dumbledore to keep her safe. Dumbledore chose to capitalise on Snape's remorse and initiated him into the Order of the Phoenix as a double agent. He also gave Snape the job of Potions Master and Head of Slytherin at Hogwarts at the tender age of 21.
</p><p>As a spy for the Order, Snape silently kept his place within the ranks of the Death Eaters, while informing Dumbledore about their movements. He also adopted the role of secret agent for Voldemort and supplied him with strategic scraps of information about the Order. The content of these reports was often dictated by Dumbledore. It is implied that Snape withheld little if any, information from Dumbledore that was relevant to the Order's success, while Snape deliberately did the opposite for Voldemort.
</p><p>Snape resented Dumbledore's secrecy and was offended by this perceived lack of faith in his abilities. However, when Snape discovered that Dumbledore had intended for Harry to die all along, he was horrified, seeing it as a calculated betrayal of Lily's memory. Dumbledore clearly underestimated the depth of Snape's feelings, and, years later, was very surprised to learn that he still maintained his devotion.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104925" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape and Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160819104925" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160819104925" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160819104925" decoding="async" width="160" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape and Dumbledore.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/26/Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160819104925" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_and_Dumbledore.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"<i>I am fortunate, extremely fortunate, that I have you, Severus...</i>"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Dumbledore became aware of Voldemort's plan to kill him. Knowing Voldemort expected <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> to fail, and assuming Snape to be Draco's successor, Dumbledore assigned Snape the task of killing him when the situation arose. Snape was genuinely reluctant to do this and even stated when Dumbledore stated that it was necessary to protect Draco's soul that his soul may very well be damaged from such an act, showing Snape had grew to genuinely care for the Headmaster. Even with the revelation of Dumbledore's true plans for Harry, Snape hesitated for a time before carrying out his mission, his face being described as holding disgust and hatred for himself for what he was about to do. Dumbledore also entrusted Snape with protecting the students once Hogwarts fell into Voldemort's control.
</p><p>In spite of their mutual trust in each other, Dumbledore never allowed Snape his coveted position as Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher. It was claimed that he did it so that Snape wouldn't experience a resurgence of "old habits". The truth may in fact be that Dumbledore believed the post to be <a href="/wiki/Jinx" title="Jinx">jinxed</a> by Lord Voldemort after <i>he</i> failed to attain the post, and this jinx had prevented any teacher from lasting beyond a year. To place Snape in such a position might have risked his safety, and Dumbledore would not have permitted such a risk, in case he required Snape's aid against Voldemort again. When Dumbledore was infected by the curse on Marvolo Gaunt's ring, he asked Snape to kill him. Knowing that such an act would vilify Snape beyond any doubt in the mind of the Wizarding public, Dumbledore allowed Snape the position because he would have to leave immediately anyway.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Petunia_Evans">Petunia Evans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Petunia Evans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Petunia Evans"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You and that Snape boy ... weirdos, that's what you two are!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Petunia Evans insulting <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">her sister</a> and Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721182515" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="216" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Petunia Dursley POA.jpg" data-image-key="Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160721182515" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721182515" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160721182515" decoding="async" width="160" height="216" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Petunia Dursley POA.jpg" data-image-key="Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20160721182515" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Petunia_Dursley_POA.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Petunia Evans</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape first met <a href="/wiki/Petunia_Dursley" title="Petunia Dursley">Petunia Evans</a> during their childhood. She was the sister of <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, but Petunia was a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a>, unlike her sister. Snape and Petunia strongly disliked each other, from the first moment they met. Petunia, who was contemptuous of anything out of the ordinary, viewed him with disdain because of his poor economic status and because he was such an oddball. Snape, on the other hand, regarded her balefully because she was a Muggle, and because she made disparaging comments about his clothes. It is unknown how Petunia reacted to (or if she even ever knew about) Snape calling Lily a <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>, but it can assumed that this incident caused Petunia to hate him even more.
</p><p>Ironically, Petunia and Snape's negative encounters with each other as children and adolescents helped lay the foundations for their respective adult personalities. It is possible that Petunia's interactions with Snape exacerbated her already growing disdain for the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">Wizarding world</a> and eventual estrangement with Lily. Likewise, Snape's antipathy towards Petunia helped fuel his dislike towards Muggles in general, causing him to experiment with <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">Pure-blood supremacy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, culminating in his recruitment in the Death Eaters. Even more tragically, Snape's actions as a Death Eater caused the death of Petunia's sister Lily to be murdered by Voldemort, which in turn caused Petunia to grudgingly adopt (and abuse and neglect) her nephew <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. 
</p><p>Years after Snape's death, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">one</a> of Petunia's great-nephews would be named after Snape. It is unknown if she had known about this, given how she likely severed contact with Harry after he left her house. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Severus Snape wasn't yours. Snape was Dumbledore's. Dumbledore's from the moment you starting hunting down my mother. And you never realised it, because of the thing you can't understand ... he loved her for nearly all of his life. </i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Lord Voldemort</b>: "<i>It matters not! It matters not whether Snape was mine or Dumbledore's, or what petty obstacles they tried to put in my path! I crushed them as I crushed your mother, Snape's supposed great love!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> regarding Snape's duplicity<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 158px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220615" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="156" height="238" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Voldemort1998.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20141122220615" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220615" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20141122220615" decoding="async" width="156" height="238" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Voldemort1998.jpg" data-image-key="Voldemort1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Voldemort1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20141122220615" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Voldemort1998.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lord Voldemort, his former master turned enemy and eventual killer</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In his days as a Death Eater, Snape was one of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s most trusted and devoted servants. In 1980, Snape overheard part of a <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">prophecy</a> foretelling Voldemort's downfall. After being caught, Snape hurried to tell Voldemort what he had heard, unaware that his information was incomplete. However, he turned against the Dark Lord the moment he decided to target <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Potter</a>.
</p><p>When Voldemort returned to physical form in 1995, Snape ostensibly returned to him as a spy for the Order. Using <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a>, Snape was able to close his mind, hide his true allegiance and maintain his cover as a faithful Death Eater. Snape was one of the only Death Eaters to have the Dark Lord's complete trust and, after he <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">murdered</a> Albus Dumbledore, he became Voldemort's most trusted adviser. He was held in such high regard that Voldemort accepted making him Headmaster of Hogwarts after seizing power.
</p><p>However, Voldemort coldly had <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">his snake</a>, Nagini, kill Snape in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, believing it would make him the true master of the <a href="/wiki/Elder_Wand" title="Elder Wand">Elder Wand</a>. Although he claimed he regretted its necessity, he felt no remorse over murdering one of his most faithful advisors. After Snape's death, Harry Potter revealed to Voldemort that Snape had managed to deceive him for years because he acted entirely out of love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> — something Voldemort neither understood or cared about. Indeed, at the time Snape asked Voldemort to spare Lily's life, he erroneously believed that Snape's interest in her was merely physical, and callously stated that there were other women "of purer blood, worthier of him" after her death. Voldemort also reacted with indifference to Snape's true loyalties, as Voldemort mistakenly believed that Snape's death made Voldemort the master of the Elder Wand. This error soon cost Voldemort his own life while ensuring that Snape's sacrifice was not in vain.
</p><p>It is possible that part of the reason Voldemort put so much trust in Snape was because he identified with his background. Both were the only children of Muggle fathers and <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> mothers (Voldemort: <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle_Senior" title="Tom Riddle Senior">Tom Riddle Snr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope Gaunt</a>; Snape: <a href="/wiki/Tobias_Snape" title="Tobias Snape">Tobias Snape</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eileen_Prince" title="Eileen Prince">Eileen Prince</a>). Both Muggle men had nothing but hatred for their sons and wives and neglected their sons and as a consequence both Riddle and Snape yearned to shed their unhappy beginnings. Voldemort's father had abandoned his wife when she was pregnant with their son, while Snape's father was abusive towards his wife and their young son. Both Riddle and Snape claimed greater identification with their maternal lineage than their paternal ancestry —the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Gaunt" title="House of Gaunt">Gaunt family</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prince_family" title="Prince family">Prince family</a>, respectively. Both men grew up in poverty — Voldemort grew up in an <a href="/wiki/Wool%27s_Orphanage" title="Wool&#39;s Orphanage">orphanage</a>, while Snape lived in <a href="/wiki/Spinner%27s_End" title="Spinner&#39;s End">Spinner's End</a>.
</p><p>In addition, both Riddle and Snape were Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>, and were known for their intelligence. Both men had a passion for the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a> and <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a> as childhood, and bestowed grandiose titles onto themselves (Riddle was known as Lord Voldemort, while Snape adopted the name the Half-Blood Prince). Both saw <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> as sort of a real home as opposed to their default home. In addition, both men kept a book related to the Dark Arts in their sixteenth years — Voldemort had the <a href="/wiki/T._M._Riddle%27s_Diary" title="T. M. Riddle&#39;s Diary">diary</a> that he converted into a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, while Snape had a <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_copy_of_Advanced_Potion-Making" title="Severus Snape&#39;s copy of Advanced Potion-Making">Potions textbook</a> that he used to write original magic. Lastly both were part of a <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_gang" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s gang">gang of fu</a><a href="/wiki/Gang_of_Slytherins" title="Gang of Slytherins">ture Death Eaters</a> who bullied their fellow students. Voldemort may have seen him as a trusted Death Eater who shared the same hatred for his father as he had for his own. The only major thing that differs between Voldemort and Snape's relationships with their fathers is murder; Voldemort had murdered his own father while Snape did <i>not</i> murder his. Voldemort must have also recognised Snape as a powerful and intelligent wizard, traits which would manifest as usefulness to his ideology.
</p><p>However, there were other differences between Snape and Voldemort. Snape had a secret love for <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> for most of his life, which motivated him to defect from the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and protect her <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">son</a> after her <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_Godric%27s_Hollow_(1981)" title="Attack at Godric&#39;s Hollow (1981)">death</a> at Voldemort's hands. Voldemort, on the other hand, disregarded love as a weakness that was beyond his comprehension, and had allegiance to only himself. This had coincidentally led to his own undoing. In addition, unlike Voldemort, Snape had known about the existence of the wizarding world before he was eleven years old (likely due to the fact that Snape's mother was actually present in his childhood).
