</p><p>Snape possessed the ability of independent flight, which was presumably taught to him by Lord Voldemort as he displayed the same ability during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>. This shows that Lord Voldemort had a great deal of trust in Snape as he taught him a very unique ability, something he might not have done with any other <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 238px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120731222117" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="236" height="164" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family Egypt holiday photograph.jpg" data-image-key="Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20120731222117" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120731222117" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20120731222117" decoding="async" width="236" height="164" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family Egypt holiday photograph.jpg" data-image-key="Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20120731222117" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family_Egypt_holiday_photograph.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Weasleys had a neutral if not unkind relationship with Snape. The Weasleys were blood-traitors, supporters of Muggles and Muggle-borns and opposed to the Dark Arts, all things Snape held opposite views towards as a Death Eater. Snape had relinquished most prejudices after switching sides though. It is unknown if Snape was still loyal to the Death Eaters when <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon Prewett</a> were killed or if he had defected before their deaths. Both events occurred in <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>. The Weasleys, like Snape in his youth, were profusely financially strained. Molly and Arthur had left Hogwarts before Snape started but knew him through their membership in the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order</a>. They seemed to, like most, trust him because Dumbledore did. Little is known about their relationship, although Molly, at least, did not let Snape's maltreatment of her children staunch her respect for him as a teacher. Given Molly was a good potioneer, this could have helped her find some common ground with him.  
</p><p>Snape taught seven Weasleys at Hogwarts. <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>, despite being Gryffindors, earned many <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.s</a>, showing Snape did not forsake his professionalism for his bias. Despite this, Ginny mentioned once that Bill and Snape did not get along when Bill was a student. There was, in fact, only a decade separating Snape and Bill. Fred and George irked Snape profusely with their pranks and disinterest in school work. Interestingly, they were their generation's <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, map and all, and as such Snape may have viewed them as a reincarnation of his childhood bullies. It is mentioned the twins got many detentions and house point losses which were likely Snape's doing.
</p><p>Ginny was the final Weasley to attend Hogwarts before Snape's death and she bared a remarkable resemblance to Lily. She was also the only remaining Weasley at Hogwarts during Snape's time as headmaster and co-lead the reformed Dumbledore's Army, unknowingly allying herself with Snape. Notably Snape seemed as worried as the other teachers when Ginny was taken into the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>.
</p><p>Ron knew of Snape's treatment of students before attending his classes, likely hearing it from an older sibling indicating a long string of antagonism between Snape and the Weasley children. Snape's murder of Dumbledore in close conjunction of Bill being maimed by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Greyback</a> and accidently maiming George gave birth to the families hatred of him. However, when the war was over, the Weasley's learned of Snape's true loyalties and likely grew to respect &amp; admire him. A new <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">member</a> of the family was eventually named for him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Malfoy_family">Malfoy family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Malfoy family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Malfoy family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Lucius always spoke highly of you.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> during Snape's class inspection<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 167px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080512050348" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="165" height="230" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Malfoys.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20080512050348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080512050348" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20080512050348" decoding="async" width="165" height="230" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Malfoys.jpg" data-image-key="Malfoys.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/77/Malfoys.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/165?cb=20080512050348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Malfoys.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius</a> and <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, whom he was on good terms with</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape appeared to be on good terms with the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy family</a>. Lucius Malfoy was a <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> when Snape began attending Hogwarts, and the two ran in the same social circles, which included other future <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. Snape and Lucius likely worked together as Death Eaters during the First Wizarding War. It's unknown if Lucius was suspicious of Snape's true allegiance, though he most likely believed Snape to be truly loyal to Voldemort. Lucius continued to think and speak well of Snape later in life. Perhaps because of this, Snape also favoured Lucius's son Draco. Draco seemed to look up to Snape, once sycophantically saying that he would make a far better Headmaster than <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Listen to me. I am trying to help you. I swore to your mother I would protect you. I made the Unbreakable Vow, Draco —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape to Draco Malfoy<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>However, after his father's imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> following the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, Draco came to resent and mistrust Snape, suspecting that he was trying to usurp his father's place in the Death Eater ranks. He refused Snape's repeated offers of help with <a href="/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Plot to assassinate Albus Dumbledore">the task</a> <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> assigned him in his sixth year. <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">Narcissa Malfoy</a>, on the other hand, begged Snape to assist Draco in his task to assassinate Dumbledore, fearing that her son was being set up to fail. She ignored the warnings of her sister, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who did not trust Snape, and had him make an <a href="/wiki/Unbreakable_Vow" title="Unbreakable Vow">Unbreakable Vow</a> to help Draco and take over the task should he fail. This speaks highly as to the trust and respect the Malfoys had for Snape.
</p><p>It's unknown how the Malfoys reacted upon learning of Snape's death and true loyalties. They were possibly saddened due to their longtime friendship. It's possible that they were also sympathetic due to their own disillusionment from Voldemort.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>I don't trust you, Snape, as you very well know!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Bellatrix Lestrange's distrust of Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 166px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="164" height="229" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140622235902" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" decoding="async" width="164" height="229" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix Lestrange promo.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/164?cb=20140622235902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix_Lestrange_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, whom he had little patience for</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Unlike her Malfoy relatives, Bellatrix Lestrange invested none of her faith in Snape. It's possible that the two got along better during the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a> as Sirius once described the two as old acquaintances; however, later in life, she showed nothing but distrust toward him. She saw right through his triple agent charade, even though <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> could not. Part of the reason for this may have been Snape's <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a> status and his avoidance of imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, while she was incarcerated there for years. Given Bellatrix's obsessive, slavish love for Voldemort, she may have envied the trust the Dark Lord put in Snape, whom she considered her inferior in both blood and service. 
</p><p>She was suspicious when Snape did not immediately return to Voldemort after his rebirth nor come to the Dark Lord's aide before that, and why he never took an opportunity to kill <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> when, as one of the boy's <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professors</a>, he had easy access to him. When Snape easily backhanded all of her accusations, bringing up that Lord Voldemort himself interrogated him of those lines, Bellatrix was lost for words; Snape was cunning enough to use the power of mere words to render Bella such, for he knew that to further her doubt of Severus would, by extension, mean that she would also be doubting the Dark Lord. And she was too fanatical to let such disparity in opinion between herself and her master go too far. With her logical reasons for distrusting Snape were gone, her irrational jealousy was all she had left to give her a reason to hate him. For that reason it perhaps grew stronger. Bellatrix was uneasy speaking openly about things around Snape, and tried to discourage her <a href="/wiki/Narcissa_Malfoy" title="Narcissa Malfoy">younger sister</a> from asking him for help with Draco's task. Although Bellatrix did not fear or respect Snape like most others did, she seemed to only avoid his bad side so as to avoid Voldemort's bad side by extention.
</p><p>Snape, on the other hand, seemed to regard Bellatrix coldly. He had very little patience for her dramatics and tendency towards hysteria. He even took the opportunity to mock her for her struggle against the six teenagers from <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, and that she was losing her status in Voldemort's eyes. Snape and Bellatrix were Voldemort's most powerful and trusted servants (or so Voldemort thought as far as Snape was concerned) and as such they never picked a real fight with one another. They were also the Death Eaters that the Order of the Phoenix and its associates hated the most and the ones the other Death Eaters feared and respected the most. Bellatrix never managed to convince anyone of Snape's true loyalty and died moments before it was revealed to everyone that she had been right all along. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Igor_Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Igor Karkaroff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Igor Karkaroff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>...don't see what there is to fuss about, Igor.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Igor Karkaroff</b>: "<i>Severus, you cannot pretend this isn't happening! It's been getting clearer and clearer for months, I am becoming seriously concerned, I can't deny it—</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Then flee. Flee, I will make your excuses. I, however, am remaining at Hogwarts.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape and Karkaroff speaking in private during the Yule Ball<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100724115703" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="242" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Igor Karkaroff GoF.jpg" data-image-key="Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20100724115703" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100724115703" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20100724115703" decoding="async" width="160" height="242" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Igor Karkaroff GoF.jpg" data-image-key="Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20100724115703" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Igor_Karkaroff_GoF.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Igor_Karkaroff" title="Igor Karkaroff">Igor Karkaroff</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape and Karkaroff had a little bit of history with each other from the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. Karkaroff was captured by <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> and during his trial, in a desperate attempt to avoid going to prison he gave to the Ministry many names of Death Eaters, including Snape. However, at the time he was not aware that Snape was a double agent. He desperately tried to convince the court that Snape remained guilty despite the judge telling him Snape was cleared.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, when Karkaroff's and Snape's Dark Marks were burning stronger, Karkaroff told his worries to Snape, who expressed little concern to him. As the year progressed, Karkaroff continued to pursue Snape over the issue, to which Snape became increasingly annoyed, and even started to evade him. Snape described Karkaroff as cowardly and had no intention of joining him in hiding once Voldemort returned. Karkaroff's death did not seem to surprise Snape.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death_Eaters">Death Eaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Death Eaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Death Eaters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>...you and your precious little Death Eater friends — you see, you don’t even deny it! You don’t even deny that’s what you’re all aiming to be! You can’t wait to join You-Know-Who, can you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Lily Evans on the day she and Snape had their falling out<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 168px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="166" height="227" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20091129164509" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20091129164509" decoding="async" width="166" height="227" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/166?cb=20091129164509" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A masked <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus became a member of the Death Eaters after <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. During his time at school, he was member of a "gang of <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a> that would later become Death Eaters". This gang included <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Avery (Marauder-era)">Avery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Marauder-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mulciber (Marauder-era)">Mulciber</a>, <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wilkes" title="Wilkes">Wilkes</a>. <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a> could not understand how he could be friends with them, as they had an "evil sense of humour". It's unknown how close he really was with the members of this gang, however he did seem somewhat defensive when Lily spoke ill of Mulciber and Avery implying a possible level of intimacy with them at least. Rosier and Wilkes were killed by Aurors after the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>; Rodolphus, Bellatrix, and Mulciber were captured (but later escaped), while Avery managed to defect. Besides Bellatrix, it's unknown what kind of relationship he had with his old school friends as an adult.
</p><p>Other Death Eaters Snape knew were <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a>, two siblings. Judging by Amycus's reaction upon seeing Snape at the Astronomy Tower it seems that he (and possibly Alecto) truly believed that Snape was on their side. Amycus and Alecto were Deputy Headmasters at Hogwarts, at the time Snape was Headmaster. They were both sadistic, and they liked to torture the students who opposed them. They also ordered the students to practise the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on punished students. Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a> appeared to be friendly with Snape too however he seemed resentful when Voldemort valued Snape's information and accomplishments over his own. Along with <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, they seemed to fear Snape's abilities, as they instantly stood down when he approached to kill Dumbledore, despite Draco being tasked with the job.
</p><p>Furthermore, Snape knew the extremely loyal Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>. during the First Wizarding War. For many years, it was believed that Barty Crouch was dead. However, he escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> and planned to send Harry Potter to Voldemort, who would be reborn. Snape, along with Dumbledore and McGonagall, saved Harry from Crouch while he was trying to kill Harry. Snape was surprised that Crouch was still alive. Later, the Death Eater was given the Dementor's Kiss though no reaction from Snape is noted.
</p><p>Other known Death Eaters were <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Augustus_Rookwood" title="Augustus Rookwood">Augustus Rookwood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nott" title="Nott">Nott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crabbe" title="Crabbe">Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goyle" title="Goyle">Goyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jugson" title="Jugson">Jugson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gibbon" title="Gibbon">Gibbon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rosier" title="Rosier">Rosier</a>, <a href="/wiki/Avery_(Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Avery (Riddle-era)">Avery</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mulciber_(Riddle-era)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mulciber (Riddle-era)">Mulciber</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lestrange" title="Lestrange">Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">Travers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>. Rodolphus and Rabastan were the only ones who tried to search for Lord Voldemort after the first defeat, along with Bellatrix and Barty Crouch Jnr During the Second Wizarding War. All those Death Eaters were either killed or imprisoned after Voldemort's final defeat. Although not shown interacting much with Snape, they all presumably held him in the same respect and fear that Yaxley &amp; Greyback did and, considering Snape's rank, had to answer to him. According to Snape some of them believed that he was not truly loyal to their cause, however none of them (save Bellatrix) openly confronted him about it.
</p><p>It is unknown how the surviving Death Eaters reacted — either as a group or as individuals — to reveal of Snape's demise (if they found out) or the revelations of his true <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">loyalties</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Possibly no one's warned you, Lupin, but this class contains Neville Longbottom. I would advise you not to entrust him with anything difficult. Not unless Miss Granger is hissing instructions in his ear.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Severus Snape insults Neville in front of the other teachers<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 158px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="156" height="243" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20140610141612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20140610141612" decoding="async" width="156" height="243" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/156?cb=20140610141612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Longbottom.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, his student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville Longbottom was perhaps one of the worst <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> students Snape ever taught. As such, Snape was especially cruel to him and often made a point of ridiculing his failures in class.<sup id="cite_ref-PS8_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS8-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COS11_48-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS11-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On one occasion, Snape threatened to test Neville's <a href="/wiki/Shrinking_Solution" title="Shrinking Solution">Shrinking Solution</a> on his <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">pet toad</a>, despite the fact that the <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">potion</a> would be poisonous if not brewed correctly. Even outside of his own classroom, Snape did not hesitate from offering harsh opinions of Neville.<sup id="cite_ref-POA7_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA7-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This treatment made Neville extremely nervous to be around Snape, and further contributed to his poor performance in <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a>. Neville admitted in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> that Snape was his greatest fear, and, predictably, Snape was the form Neville's <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> took at that time.<sup id="cite_ref-POA7_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA7-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Soon Snape heard about Neville's boggart and treated him, if possible, even worse than he usually did.<sup id="cite_ref-POA7_69-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA7-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> However, in 1996, Snape alerted members of the Order of the Phoenix, in order to save Neville, Harry and their friends from Death Eaters. Although Snape helped save Neville's life, he continued to treat him poorly in school. Neville was surprised that Snape killed Dumbledore but did learn the truth later. Snape chose to do a subtle favour for Neville when he was caught along with Ginny Weasley and Luna Lovegood attempting to steal the Sword of Gryffindor. Snape chose to send Neville, Luna and Ginny to detention with their friend Hagrid rather than subject them to the sadistic forms of discipline practised by the Carrows. When Neville killed Nagini, he inadvertently avenged Snape's murder.
</p><p>Though it is possible that from <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>'s first prophecy that it was either Neville or Harry who was to threaten Voldemort, that as a result with Voldemort going for the Potters, that Neville represented his guilt from revealing the prophecy to Voldemort and the potential alternative for what could've happened. As a result. from Snape's point of view, Neville embodied all of this and that made him detest and bully him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minerva_McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>And Potter — do try and win, won’t you? Or <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">we’ll</a> be out of the running for the eighth year in a row, as Professor Snape was kind enough to remind me only last night...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape's friendly <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> rivarly with McGonagall<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 161px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="159" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20150810172040" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20150810172040" decoding="async" width="159" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/159?cb=20150810172040" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, his colleague and former professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was generally on good professional terms with Snape. However, seeing as Snape was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a>, while McGonagall was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Gryffindor_House" title="Head of Gryffindor House">Head of Gryffindor House</a>, there was some antagonism between them, as Snape usually teased McGonagall when Slytherin had more points than Gryffindor. McGonagall was also wary of the fact that Snape was once a Death Eater. However, she trusted him because she knew that Dumbledore trusted him, too. She also did not hesitate to call him out when she believed he was being too cruel. McGonagall, like Snape, was very strict, but much more fair, as noted by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. McGonagall was Snape's Transfiguration professor when he was a student and likely admired his brilliance.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Coward! COWARD!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;McGonagall attempts to apprehend Snape after he flees the castle during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Her trust of Snape evaporated after <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>'s murder. Furthermore, when Snape became Headmaster of Hogwarts, McGonagall tried to oppose him and the Carrows, without knowing that Snape was trying to protect the students from the Carrows, too. When the war was coming to a head, she personally attacked Snape and violently called him a coward, a trait she, as Head Of Gryffindor, loathed. It is unknown how she reacted when she learned about his true loyalties, but it is likely that she forgave him. She permitted <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape%27s_portrait" title="Severus Snape&#39;s portrait">his portrait</a> to be hung in the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Headmaster&#39;s office">Headmaster's office</a>, at Harry's request.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Snape... we all wondered... but he trusted... always... </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Professor McGonagall after Dumbledore's death<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest?cb=20100310181520" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="257" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter.png" data-image-key="20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest?cb=20100310181520" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" decoding="async" width="150" height="257" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="20100111183429!Flitwick HBPoster Lighter.png" data-image-key="20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c6/20100111183429%21Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100310181520" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:20100111183429!Flitwick_HBPoster_Lighter.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, his colleague and former professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape was respected professionally among his colleagues at Hogwarts. Though many of them exhibited some wariness towards him due to his status as a former Death Eater, they opted to trust him because Dumbledore did. When Snape killed Dumbledore, however, the entire staff was shocked. In 1998, Flitwick and Sprout, like many other teachers, tried to oppose Snape and the Carrows, and they were among the ones who chased Snape out of Hogwarts before the battle. Flitwick and Sprout were Snape's Charms and Herbology teachers respectively in the latter's youth.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I’m tellin’ yeh, yer wrong! I don’ know why Harry’s broom acted like that, but Snape wouldn’ try an’ kill a student!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Rubeus Hagrid defending Snape to Hermione Granger<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> was no friend of Snape's but trusted him, mainly because Dumbledore trusted him and would always defend him whenever Harry or Ron would express their distrust for him. Both Hagrid and Snape became members of the first and second <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and they both fought against Voldemort. When Snape killed Dumbledore, Hagrid initially disbelieved the fact and told Harry he must be mistaken but was later furious to learn that Snape had indeed killed the late Headmaster. Hagrid openly opposed Snape when he became the Headmaster of Hogwarts by holding a <a href="/wiki/Support_Harry_Potter_party" title="Support Harry Potter party">Support Harry Potter party</a> (unaware Snape was secretly still on their side), an act which almost resulted in his arrest and forced him to go into hiding until the final battle. Before Hagrid fled, Snape put students in detentions with Hagrid, ensuring that they were protected from the harsher and torturous punishments from the Carrows. However, Hagrid eventually learned of Snape's true loyalties during the final confrontation of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 162px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121226172917" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="160" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Horace Slughorn.jpg" data-image-key="Horace_Slughorn.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20121226172917" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121226172917" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20121226172917" decoding="async" width="160" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Horace Slughorn.jpg" data-image-key="Horace_Slughorn.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e0/Horace_Slughorn.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/160?cb=20121226172917" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Horace_Slughorn.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, Severus's Head of House and Potions Professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape disliked most of the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> instructors, such as <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>. Though this was at least partially out of his own desire to teach the subject, he had legitimate reasons to dislike them, as Quirrell was an agent of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, Lockhart was a narcissistic fraud, Lupin had acted as a bystander to, if not directly participating in, much of the bullying Snape faced in his school days, and Umbridge was a corrupt woman who wanted the entire school under her thumb. The only <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor Snape refrained from displaying disrespect to was <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Jnr</a> impersonating <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>, the toughest <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> hunter the Ministry ever had. Harry surmised this was out of fear, but it was more likely due to allegiance. It should be noted that Moody had been the one to kill <a href="/wiki/Evan_Rosier" title="Evan Rosier">Evan Rosier</a>, an old friend of Snape's, and possibly others. 
</p><p>Horace Slughorn had been Snape's Potions master and head of house. Snape was made a member of the Slug Club as he was a brilliant student and even then his potion abilities were almost as good if not equal to Slughorn's. Snape might have been the student to whom Slughorn once award a vial of Liquid Luck. It is highly unlikely that Slughorn was aware of Snape's self-altered textbook and was flabbergasted when Snape murdered Dumbledore.  
</p><p>Snape seemed on good terms with <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, the caretaker, who respected Snape, and like him, disliked most students at Hogwarts. Snape often had Filch report directly to him if he found anything suspicious during his nighttime patrols. It's possible that after Voldemort took over Filch was only able to remain at Hogwarts because of his loyalty towards Snape. It is unknown how Filch reacted when he learned that Snape killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>, or when Snape himself died.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_students">Hogwarts students</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts students">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Hogwarts students"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Before we begin today’s lesson, I think it appropriate to remind you that next June you will be sitting an important examination, during which you will prove how much you have learned about the composition and use of magical potions. Moronic though some of this class undoubtedly are, I expect you to scrape an ‘<a href="/wiki/Acceptable" title="Acceptable">Acceptable</a>’ in your O.W.L., or suffer my... displeasure.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape speaking to <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">fifth year</a> students in Potions<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="160" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="240" height="160" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Some of Snape's students</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape was not popular among the majority of the students at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. He was quite strict and had high standards. He refused to allow any students into his <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level Potions classes unless they achieved an "O" grade on their O.W.L. exam for the subject (many other Hogwarts teachers would still accept the next-best grade, "E", for their advanced classes). Despite N.E.W.T.s not beginning until the sixth-year, it was Snape's policy to grade his fifth-year students by the N.E.W.T. scale. At the beginning of the 1995-1996 school year, he warned his fifth-year students that he expected everyone to make some sort of passing grade on their O.W.L. exams, even if they were not intending to try for his N.E.W.T. class. Anyone who made a poor grade would deal with his "displeasure".
</p><p>In addition to being strict, he was not always fair. His having been bullied so much as a child may have fuelled his oppressiveness as a teacher. During Harry Potter's years at the school, Snape particularly enjoyed taking points from Harry's House, Gryffindor. He generally favoured the students in his own House, Slytherin, including Draco Malfoy. However, he was still irritated if they did not live up to his expectations and would punish them too. On at least one occasion, he gave Crabbe and Goyle detention because they had failed their O.W.L. exam for Defence Against the Dark Arts. He also had no qualms punishing Merula Snyde for attempting to frame Jacob's sibling despite her being a Slytherin and seems to dislike her for being perhaps the most atrocious liar and blamer among Slytherins. The students of his house generally regarded him with respect and pride, even cheering loudly when he effortlessly defeated Lockhart with one spell. However, becoming the Defence Against the Dark Arts teacher made Snape fairer (if only slightly) as he lowered his standards to allow more students to enter advanced studies, and he taught the lectures with more passion that intrigued his students' interests.
</p><p>Although he disliked most students, a feeling that is quite mutual, he was not truly evil and did felt quite a lot of concern for their safety and well-being. After Rowan Khanna's tragic murder at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a> rendered the student body devastated and mournful during the <a href="/wiki/1989%E2%80%931990_school_year" title="1989–1990 school year">1989–1990 school year</a>, Snape proceeded to teach his <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth years</a> how to concoct the <a href="/wiki/Potion_for_Dreamless_Sleep" title="Potion for Dreamless Sleep">Dreamless Sleep Potion</a> in <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions class</a>, due in part to many of his students suffering from sleep-deprived nights following Khanna's death. He was also noted to be particularly patient by <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a> during that specific Potions class, sympathising with the grief his class felt and patiently urging them to focus on his lesson.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, when Professor McGonagall informed the staff that a student had been captured by the monster from the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, Snape displayed a hint of genuine concern by gripping the back of a chair very hard.<sup id="cite_ref-COS16_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS16-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> He also did everything he could to protect the students from Voldemort's control of Hogwarts, while Alecto and Amycus Carrow were appointed at the school, further showing he did care for his students even if he rarely showed it.<sup id="cite_ref-DH33_7-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH33-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix_members">Order of the Phoenix members</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=45" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix members">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix members"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>Git.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>He's on our side now.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>He's still a git.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Fred and Hermione about Snape's behaviour towards them<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20150206155602" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150206155602" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20150206155602" decoding="async" width="251" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix – first generation.jpg" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix_–_first_generation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d0/Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20150206155602" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix_%E2%80%93_first_generation.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Snape's relationships with some members of the Order of the Phoenix have already been established: <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily Evans</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Marauders" title="Marauders">Marauders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>.
</p><p>Snape was not particularly gracious towards <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, probably because she was so close to Remus Lupin. When they met at school in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, he maliciously said "I was interested to see your new Patronus. I think you were better off with the old one... the new one looks weak." Snape did, however, respect Tonks' abilities as he was her Potions master whilst she was a Hogwarts student and she earned an O in her O.W.L. This is evident as he never let one with a lesser grade take the N.E.W.T which was a requirement to be an auror. Tonks was shocked when Snape killed Dumbledore and never learned that Snape was on their side, as she was killed by Bellatrix Lestrange during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. 
</p><p>Snape had a mixed relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a>. While he disliked their children, he seemed to be on civil terms with <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly</a>. However, when he murdered Dumbledore, the Weasley family obviously turned against him. Snape also accidentally cursed off George's ear, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, while he was trying to hit another Death Eater. The Weasley family learned that Snape was on their side in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, except Fred, who was killed in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>He also did not much care for a fellow member of the Order <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>, who was also a thief. In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a> he was arrested for impersonating an <a href="/wiki/Inferius" title="Inferius">Inferius</a>. When <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a> asked Snape about it, he answered that the "Inferius" was, in fact, <i>a smelly sneak thief named Mundungus Fletcher</i>. It is most likely that Mundungus learned that Snape was on their side after the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p><p>It is likely that the members of the Order who survived the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> were told by Harry of Snape's true loyalties.
</p>
<h3><span id="Jacob's_sibling"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Jacob.27s_sibling">Jacob's sibling</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=46" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Jacob&#039;s sibling">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Jacob&#039;s sibling"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery"><b>Snape</b>: "<i>I wanted anyone watching to believe that we were at odds...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Jacob's sibling</b>: "<i>Aren't we <b>always</b> at odds?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Snape and Jacob's sibling<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200428175803" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="225" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jacob&#39;s sibling generic.png" data-image-key="Jacob&#39;s_sibling_generic.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200428175803" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200428175803" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200428175803" decoding="async" width="180" height="225" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jacob&#39;s sibling generic.png" data-image-key="Jacob&#39;s_sibling_generic.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200428175803" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jacob%27s_sibling_generic.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Much like for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, Snape seemed to harbour a particular dislike for <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">Jacob's sibling</a>. He first met the student when they were having a quarrel with the imperious <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> <a href="/wiki/Merula_Snyde" title="Merula Snyde">Merula Snyde</a> outside <a href="/wiki/Potions_classroom" class="mw-redirect" title="Potions classroom">his dungeon</a>, and callously dismissed their reason for arguing with her in defence of their best friend <a href="/wiki/Rowan_Khanna" title="Rowan Khanna">Rowan Khanna</a>. Due to the sordid reputation of <a href="/wiki/Jacob_(Hogwarts_student)" title="Jacob (Hogwarts student)">their brother</a> casting much apprehension over both the staff and student body, Snape was initially mistrustful of them and made no attempt to hide his contempt for Jacob's sibling during their first-ever <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions class</a>. When their potion was egregiously sabotaged by Merula, Snape's disdain for them was exacerbated, with him unfairly deducting 10 <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">House points</a> from them as punishment for their supposed incompetence. He continued to mistreat them even further after their unsanctioned duel with Merula, being largely dismissive of who instigated the fight but unreasonably assuming that Jacob's sibling was the one who started it. His dislike for them was great enough that he unsuccessful appealed to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> for their immediate expulsion from Hogwarts, and, disregarding the fact that his aforementioned Slytherin student also had her own part to play in the duel, cruelly subtracted an additional 20 House points from Jacob's sibling soon after. 
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">"<i>Time to stir my <a href="/wiki/Cauldron" title="Cauldron">cauldron</a>. I bet Snape could do this with his eyes closed.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Jacob's sibling's adoration of Snape's abilities as a <a href="/wiki/Potioneer" title="Potioneer">Potioneer</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter:_Hogwarts_Mystery" title="Harry Potter: Hogwarts Mystery">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>The student in question, however, was always courteous and civil towards Snape, going so far as to openly acknowledge the latter as being an exceptional teacher on the infrequent occasions that he wasn't berating them, with Snape gradually finding himself to begrudgingly acknowledge said student's flair for potion-making. Indeed, Jacob's sibling only ever betrayed signs of impatience or anger whenever Snape became particularly derisive and scornful, with them thus forming a semi-antagonistic relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> over the years. 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Patricia_Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=47" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Patricia Rakepick">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Patricia Rakepick"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest?cb=20180827165324" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="276" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery.png" data-image-key="Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180827165324" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest?cb=20180827165324" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180827165324" decoding="async" width="180" height="276" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Patricia Rakepick - Hogwarts Mystery.png" data-image-key="Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180827165324" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Patricia_Rakepick_-_Hogwarts_Mystery.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Patricia_Rakepick" title="Patricia Rakepick">Patricia Rakepick</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Five years his senior at Hogwarts, Severus Snape met Patricia Rakepick for the first time while they were both still students, and took an immediate dislike to her: Bold as brass and with little regards for school rules, and a member of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a> to boot, Patricia Rakepick was someone whom Severus would one day compare to his arch-rival during his schooldays, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a>, another trouble-making Gryffindor. Whilst it is uncertain what he thought of Rakepick's initial claims about the existence of the fabled Cursed Vaults as a student, he did acknowledge that she was remarkably ambitious for a Gryffindor, and by no means stupid. By the time he had replaced <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> as the school's <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a>, Rakepick was already a notable curse-breaker and building her career on eliminating her competition. Wary of her true intentions, when Albus Dumbledore invited her back to help break the curses plaging the school and its denizens, their old rivalry immediately reignited, and Snape immediately went about trying to uncover whatever ulterior motives she might have, suspecting that she wanted to use the vaults to take control of Hogwarts.
</p><p>From that moment on, it is known that Snape and Rakepick were engaging in a subtle battle of wits, and even used students to spy on one another. Recognising that Rakepick regarded <a href="/wiki/Jacob%27s_sibling" title="Jacob&#39;s sibling">one of the pupils</a> as a potential rival in her quest to find the vaults, and aware how Rakepick dealt with rivals, Snape cleverly had said student serving as his spy to shift her attention over on him to protect the student as a supposed mastermind of the youngster's actions, while also using the ploy as a tool to try and learn what Rakepick was up to and expose her to Dumbledore, the one person whom they knew for a certainty would be able to put a stop to her plot, whatever it might be.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=48" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Media"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=49" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>Severus</i> means "stern" in <a href="/wiki/Latin" title="Latin">Latin</a>, and is the root of the English word "severe".<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> It was a <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Roman">Roman</a> cognomen, common to members of the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Severan_dynasty" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Severan dynasty">Severan dynasty</a> of Emperors, including one notorious for his harsh persecution of the early Christians.
</p><p>Septimius Severus, also known as Severus, was Roman Emperor from 193 to 211. As a young man, he advanced through the customary succession of offices under the reigns of Marcus Aurelius and Commodus. Severus seized power after the death of Emperor Pertinax in 193 during the Year of the Five Emperors. After deposing and killing the incumbent emperor Didius Julianus, Severus fought his rival claimants, the generals Pescennius Niger (possibly <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a>) and Clodius Albinus (<a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>). Niger was defeated in 194 at the Battle of Issus in Cilicia. Later that year Severus waged a short punitive campaign beyond the eastern frontier, annexing the Kingdom of Osroene as a new province. Severus defeated Albinus three years later at the Battle of Lugdunum in Gaul.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> has said that she took the surname Snape from an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a> village<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> in <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Suffolk" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Suffolk">Suffolk</a>. There is also a village called "<i>Snape</i>" in <a href="/wiki/Yorkshire" title="Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a>, which was rebuilt by the aforementioned emperor, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Septimus_Severus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Septimus Severus">Septimus Severus</a>. Snape is also an English verb meaning "to be hard upon, rebuke, snub", derived from the Old Norse "<i>sneypa"</i>, "to outrage, dishonour, disgrace".<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Interestingly J.K. Rowling used to live in Clapham Junction at the time of her starting to write the first book. Opposite Clapham Junction station is a road named Severus Road, though it is unknown if this is simply a coincidence.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?veaction=edit&amp;section=50" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape?action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span>"<i>Well, that is Snape’s tragedy. Given his time over again he would not have become a Death Eater, but like many insecure, vulnerable people (like Wormtail) he craved membership of something big and powerful, something impressive. He wanted Lily and he wanted Mulciber too. He never really understood Lily’s aversion; he was so blinded by his attraction to the dark side he thought she would find him impressive if he became a real Death Eater.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="http://www.the-leaky-cauldron.org/2007/7/30/j-k-rowling-web-chat-transcript">2007 Web Chat Transcript</a></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
