<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Snape_Pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190506191136" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape Pop.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_Pop.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Snape_Pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190506191136" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Snape_Pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190506191136" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Snape_Pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190506191136" decoding="async" width="180" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape Pop.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_Pop.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Snape_Pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190506191136" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_Pop.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as a <a href="/wiki/POP!_Vinyl" title="POP! Vinyl">POP! Vinyl</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200919203127" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="181" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape Yule Ball pop vinyl.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200919203127" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200919203127" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200919203127" decoding="async" width="180" height="181" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape Yule Ball pop vinyl.jpg" data-image-key="Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b9/Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200919203127" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_Yule_Ball_pop_vinyl.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape (in his <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> robes) as a <a href="/wiki/POP!_Vinyl" title="POP! Vinyl">POP! Vinyl</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Snape is the only known Death Eater who could conjure a <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a>.</li>
<li>Snape attended Hogwarts exactly twenty years before Harry Potter.</li>
<li>Snape came very close to receiving <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Merlin" title="Order of Merlin">Order of Merlin</a>, First Class for subduing <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>It was because of Snape that Harry Potter became aware and practical of the Disarming Charm (<i>Expelliarmus</i>). Snape used it in the introduction of the Duelling Club while duelling with Gilderoy Lockhart. He said that students should learn to disarm their opponents.</li>
<li>Severus and Lily were also close in age. They were born in the same month and year. He was only 21 days older than her.</li>
<li>Severus Snape is portrayed by the late <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Alan_Rickman" title="Alan Rickman">Alan Rickman</a> in all of the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a>, making him one of the 14 characters to appear in all eight film adaptations.
<ul><li>Rickman was Rowling's first choice for the role. Actor <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Roth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tim Roth">Tim Roth</a> was initially offered the role but turned it down to work in <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Burton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tim Burton">Tim Burton</a>'s <a href="/wiki/2001" title="2001">2001</a> film <i>Planet of the Apes</i>. Rickman was cast later on.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In the film adaptations, Severus appears to be rather older than he is in the original books, being in his early thirties at the time of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>. Alan Rickman was fifty-four when he was first cast for the role.
<ul><li>Due to the age difference between Rickman and Snape, as he is portrayed in the book, make-up was used on Rickman to make him look younger.</li></ul></li>
<li>It appears that he also played his part very well. Rupert Grint admitted to being afraid of him in an interview.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alec_Hopkins" title="Alec Hopkins">Alec Hopkins</a> plays a young Snape in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Benedict_Clarke" title="Benedict Clarke">Benedict Clarke</a> plays an even younger Snape in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Rickman died of cancer on <a href="/wiki/14_January" title="14 January">14 January</a>, <a href="/wiki/2016" title="2016">2016</a> - only five days after what would have been Snape's 56th birthday.</li></ul></li>
<li>Rickman had conversations with Rowling about his character and is one of the few Harry Potter actors that she spoke to prior to the completion of the book series about the future direction of the character. "<i>He knew very early on that he'd been in love with Lily</i>," said Rowling. "<i>He needed to understand [...] where this bitterness towards this boy who's the living example of her preference for another man came from.</i>" Rickman used this knowledge of Snape's ultimate loyalties throughout the films by deciding how to play certain scenes, deliver specific lines, or using body language to convey specific emotions. When the directors of the films would ask him why he was doing a scene a certain way or delivering a line in a specific manner, Rickman would simply reply that he knew something they did not.</li>
<li>Much like <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, Snape's character is altered to appear more likeable in the films than in the books. He does not openly insult or harass his students, with the exception of shoving or whacking Harry and Ron on the head to make them focus on their studies, and once when Ron sniggered when Umbridge was embarrassing him. He is notably less cruel to Harry than in the books, such as wishing him good luck on his first Quidditch match and even flashing him a slight smile, along with a sarcastic compliment on Harry's defeat of the mountain troll earlier that year.<sup id="cite_ref-PSf8_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSf8-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> He initially defended him, Ron, and Hermione in the second film from Filch's accusations when Mrs Norris was petrified, though he did note that there was a set of suspicious circumstances. Additionally, in the final film, when he talks with Dumbledore after revealing the Prophecy to Voldemort, he asks him to protect the entire Potter family, rather than only Lily, without Dumbledore having to prompt him to do so. Snape is also slightly more laid back and less antisocial in the films. An example is when, in the third film, he gestured Harry out of the Shrieking Shack with his head rather than verbally instructing him to leave.</li>
<li>Despite his status as a Death Eater as well as implications that he had some form of status among them before Voldemort's attack on the Potters, Snape did not seem to be aware of Peter Pettigrew's role in the Death Eaters nor was he aware that Peter was actually the one who betrayed Lily to Voldemort as he seemed sure that Sirius Black was the culprit.</li>
<li>It's likely however that he learned the truth following Voldemort's rebirth as he showed much less hostility towards Sirius than before (while still a significant amount) and he was made aware that Peter was alive and on the side of the Death Eaters.  This would likely explain his hostility towards Peter in <i>The</i> <i>Half-Blood Prince.</i></li>
<li>It is unclear why Snape is still alive in the alternate reality where Voldemort won the wizarding war, given that Voldemort should have still killed him as he believed that Snape was the master of the Elder Wand and still desired to become the wand's master.</li>
<li>During one of the sneak missions in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (video game)">PS1 version</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, Snape actually says <i>"There is something very special in the Forbidden Corridor that I've had my eye on for some time. We can't let anyone interfere with my plans. Can we, Mr Filch?"</i> as to confuse the player about who is looking for the Stone, although the line ultimately does not make much sense. However, one can interpret it as a way of bullying <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> into aiding him to protect the Stone from <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirrell</a>.</li>
<li>In the books, Snape is one of the youngest teachers to be recruited at Hogwarts school. Having taught at Hogwarts for fourteen years in <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry's fifth year</a>, Snape has been teaching Potions since he was twenty-one (it should be noted that when <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> applied for the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> post when he was eighteen, <a href="/wiki/Armando_Dippet" title="Armando Dippet">Armando Dippet</a>, then the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmaster</a>, rejected him on the basis that he was too young, although he invited him to reapply in a few years' time).<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Grudge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008205813" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="148" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Grudge.jpg" data-image-key="Grudge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Grudge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20111008205813" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Grudge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008205813" class="image"><img alt="" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Grudge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Mary_GrandPr%C3%A9" title="Mary GrandPré">Mary GrandPré</a> illustrates Snape perusing the Marauder's Map</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li>The chapter illustrations by <a href="/wiki/Mary_GrandPr%C3%A9" title="Mary GrandPré">Mary GrandPré</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">American</a> editions depict Snape with a thin goatee.</li>
<li>In the book, Nagini kills Snape by sinking her fangs into his neck after being released from her protective bubble. In the film adaptation, Lord Voldemort slashes Snape's throat, then orders Nagini to finish him off. Surprisingly, less blood is shown than in the book. This was likely due to the film's PG-13 rating.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)</a></i>, a scene with Snape was added when Lupin turned into a werewolf: instead of being unconscious as he was in the book, Snape regains his consciousness and goes to look for Harry with the intent of punishing him for his attack on him. When he hears Lupin roaring behind him and turns to find him transformed into a werewolf, Snape proves his great courage by shielding Harry, Ron and Hermione with his own body, taking a vicious slash from Lupin as a result.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Chapter 2 (<i>A Peck of Owls</i>), J.K. Rowling includes a bit of misdirection. After Petunia has revealed her knowledge of Dementors, she explains that she "<i>heard -- that awful boy --telling her about them -- years ago.</i>" Both Harry and the reader assume that "that awful boy" is referring to James Potter. However, Snape's memories later reveal that it was a conversation between him and Lily Evans that Petunia overheard, and Snape was, in fact, "that awful boy." This is the first mention in the books of a relationship between Snape and Lily, but the reader has no way of knowing that until later.</li>
<li>Amongst Severus Snape's possessions that he kept at his home was a curious object called a <a href="/wiki/Dark_Curio" title="Dark Curio">Dark Curio</a>, though the object was only ever named such in the original script for the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a> was cut from the film adaptations of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>. Hence, it is unclear how Snape located Harry and Hermione in the <a href="/wiki/Forest_of_Dean" title="Forest of Dean">Forest of Dean</a>. However, in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, as Neville is leading Harry, Ron, and Hermione in the secret passage Neville states that they "hardly see him," so in that time he could have searched over Britain to find them and give them the sword.<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190919104149" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Snape death.gif" data-image-key="Snape_death.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190919104149" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190919104149" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190919104149" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Snape death.gif" data-image-key="Snape_death.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/13/Snape_death.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190919104149" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Snape_death.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Severus' death in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>:
<ul><li>Snape's death takes place in the school's <a href="/wiki/Boathouse" title="Boathouse">Boathouse</a> rather than the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>. The art director of the series, Andrew Ackland-Snow, said in an interview with Cine Premier Mexico: "<i>We wanted to change a bit where Snape dies. In the book, he dies in the Shrieking Shack, and we wanted to get him out from, not a conventional interior, but from that kind of box, to do it in a more dramatic atmosphere. We asked [Rowling] if she agreed for that to happen in there and she loved it ... Snape dies in an extremely good way, I gotta say."</i><sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>While Harry is facing Voldemort, he calls Snape "Professor Snape". This is the first time that he addresses him with the title other than in his presence which shows that he has forgiven and even come to respect Snape for his courage and his sacrifices. One notable factor of the books was when Harry was speaking about Snape with Dumbledore, the latter would always ask Harry to address him as "Professor Snape".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Steve_Kloves" title="Steve Kloves">Steve Kloves</a> added a new scene to Snape's memories in which Snape visits Godric's Hollow shortly after Voldemort's arrival and collapses when he finds Lily's lifeless body among the wreckage in the house.</li></ul></li>
<li>When <a href="/wiki/Jany_Temime" title="Jany Temime">Jany Temime</a> took over the role of costume designer for the films, many of the characters' wardrobes were re-designed, but Snape's costume remained unchanged throughout all eight films, as Temime thought the existing costume, consisting of a black robe, worked well with Snape's character.</li>
<li>Snape is the catalyst for the entire series, since it was he who told Voldemort of the prophecy and begged Voldemort to spare Lily, enabling her to sacrifice her life for Harry, thus enabling the protection that protected Harry for so long and ultimately led to Voldemort's death.</li>
<li>Snape's character was loosely inspired by an unpleasant chemistry teacher J.K. Rowling had in secondary school, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Lawrence_Nettleship" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Lawrence Nettleship">John Lawrence Nettleship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Nettleship_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nettleship-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When asked what Snape smelled like, <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> answered: "<i>Bitterness and old shoes.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-bitternessandoldshoes_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bitternessandoldshoes-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>According to Rowling, Dumbledore never did anything about Snape's behaviour in class because "<i>Dumbledore believes there are all sorts of lessons in life... and horrible teachers are one of them.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>, when asked if she considers Snape a hero, she said she thinks of him as an extremely flawed anti-hero, stating that though he was quite cold and spiteful and a bit of a bully, he was capable of love and was immensely brave.</li>
<li>J.K. Rowling stated that Lily Evans may have grown to love Snape romantically if he was not so drawn to the Dark Arts.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Snape's actor Alan Rickman's first and middle initials - <b>Alan Sidney Patrick </b>- spell the word "asp", a type of snake, the emblem of Slytherin. Those initials are also shared with Albus Severus Potter, whose middle name is Harry Potter's tribute to one of the "bravest men he ever knew."</li>
<li>Snape and James Potter's respective actors - Alan Rickman and <a href="/wiki/Adrian_Rawlins" title="Adrian Rawlins">Adrian Rawlins</a> - shared the same first and last initials.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130211010315" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="112" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Benedict Cumberbatch Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130211010315" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130211010315" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130211010315" decoding="async" width="180" height="112" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Benedict Cumberbatch Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130211010315" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Benedict_Cumberbatch_Snape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Snape as shown in <i>The Simpsons</i> episode "Love is a Many-Splintered Thing"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Snape once made an appearance in an episode of the TV show <i>The Simpsons</i>, in which he was voiced by actor Benedict Cumberbatch.</li>
<li>A new species of crab has been named after Snape, <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harryplax" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Harryplax">Harryplax</a> Severus</i>. The name was chosen because the crab had managed to elude rediscovery for two decades after its initial discovery, like how Snape was able to hide the most important part of the story for years.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
